Suzhou

Detailed Account of Wang Wusheng's Escape from Danger 146

Following Water Police 8th Route Bandit Suppression Team Leader Wang Wusheng's escape from Taihu Lake, details of the events are given below: The lake bandits were divided into the Haizhou gang and the Henan gang. The leader of the Haizhou gang was Zhong Zhaokui, also known as Haizhou Laoba, age 30, with thick eyebrows and a narrow face, and a lean and agile body. He had committed major crimes in Tongcheng, Anhui, and other places. He had 18 boats, 160 men, and complete firearms. The Henan gang was led by Liu Ada and Zhang Kuzi, with 70 men in 10 boats. The bandits wore uniforms and had both long and short guns, as well as military flags and bugles. Zhong's gang had two inspectors, two secretaries, and three fake battalion commanders. Last month, after looting two steamships, the bandit boats gathered at Nanku that night, totaling 28 boats. While passing Miaotou, they captured Hu Rongshan and Zhang Si, Zhejiang detectives, and found two official documents on them. They were shot dead in Nanku and then their boats were dismantled and hidden in the reeds. The bandit boats traveled covertly at night, and their range was around Majia Dang, Xin Kai Lu, Hengshan, Caogang, Nanku, Hengxu, and Da Caogang. After Wang was captured, he was held on a boat of the Henan gang. Zheng Xin, son of the commander of the Dongshan Self-Defense Corps, was also captured and held by the Henan gang. Zhong Zhaokui, fearing pursuit by the police, considered killing Wang three times, but the Henan gang dissuaded him, hoping to use him to pressure the police. The Henan gang was weaker than the Haizhou gang and was often suppressed. For example, in past lootings, the Henan gang received one share for each gun, while the Haizhou gang received double. Zhong was stubborn and brutal, killing without hesitation. One day, when the bandit gang ran out of food, the Henan gang planned to go to Nanku to buy food. Zhong, fearing attention from the police, forbade it. The Henan gang eventually sent Liu Gong and two other bandits. Zhong immediately ordered them to be shot dead. As a result, the relationship between the two gangs had already turned sour. Before the water police's 7th and 8th teams engaged in a firefight with the bandits, the bandits at Xinwei (i.e., Tiandatan) saw a large fishing boat approaching from the northwest, followed by numerous small boats. Zhong knew something was amiss and told those around him that the "dogs" (bandits referred to police as dogs) were coming. But he said they were not afraid and ordered the men to raise the flags and bugles, ready to resist, saying they would seize their weapons. He then said they could "shake" Wang Wusheng (bandit slang for killing). The Henan gang hesitated slightly, but Zhong drew his short gun and fired at Wang from across the boat. Because the boats were moving at that time, the aim was inaccurate, and the bullet went straight to a bandit leader in the Henan gang. The bandit leader was shocked and quickly dodged, but a group standing next to him was killed. The bandit leader was enraged, believing that Zhong was deliberately seeking revenge. He released Wang, tied him to the boat, found a box of ammunition, gave it to Wang, and gave Zheng Xin a tube gun, ordering the two to shoot at the Haizhou gang with the other bandits. Wang, finding it inconvenient to fight in the water, ordered the Henan bandits to go ashore together. The bandit gang consisted of fifty-two men. Wang, leaning against the embankment, fired non-stop. At the same time, the water police, fighting the Haizhou gang, were joined by the boats of the 11th, 14th and 15th teams led by Captain Huai, and a "triangular battle" ensued. As a result, the Haizhou gang was defeated, outnumbered and attacked from two sides. The fifty-two men of the Henan gang, realizing that they could no longer cooperate with Zhong, immediately disbanded. Wang and Zheng found a boat and sailed away, intending to return to Wujiang, but the police of the other teams, suspecting that Wang and others were bandits, chased after them, firing bullets like rain. Wang did not have time to distinguish them and suspected that the water police were bandits (because the boats used by the water police were often disguised, and the bandits also wore uniforms). He only ordered the small boat to move forward quickly. Because the boat was slow, the bullets came closer and closer, so they abandoned it and walked, swimming across a river to Nanku, and then wading across another river to reach Wujiang at about 4 pm on the 4th. Later, the water police found four incomplete corpses floating in Taihu Lake near Xinkai Lu. Upon close examination, they were identified as two men and two women. The female corpses had small feet and were naked from the waist up. Their chests and abdomens had been cut open, and their hearts had been removed. One corpse was headless, and the heads and hands of the two male corpses had been cut off. The scene was horrifying. District Chief Gong returned to Suzhou on the night of the 5th, and Wang also returned with him. He reported the situation to the Second District Department in Suzhou and then went to Wuxi. The water police of the 2nd District, 9th, 10th and 6th brigades entered Taihu Lake to assist the 3rd District water police in searching for the fleeing bandits and rescuing the remaining hostages.

Wuxi

Panic Over Sudden Rise in Rice Prices Again 151

Since the beginning of spring, the rice price in Wuxi has been gradually rising uncontrollably, causing panic among the common people who live on grains. Until recently, a week ago, due to the arrival of new Ke Xian rice and foreign rice in large quantities, the rice price continued to fall. High-quality white rice fell to 16.23 yuan per shi. Unexpectedly, the rice price has suddenly risen again in the past few days. Yesterday, the opening price of No. 1 high-quality white rice was 17.7 yuan, small ground rice was 14.7 yuan, and Saigon rice was 16.23 yuan. It is heard that the reason for this increase is the scarcity of goods and the strong sales in Shanghai. The unscrupulous merchants who hoard and speculate are all overjoyed.

Police Arresting People at Night Causes Trouble 152

Tang Yingchuan, a farmer from Qianxiang Village, Fuzhou Township, 15th District, had a quarrel with his clansman Tang Fugen this summer and filed a complaint with the county government accusing Fugen of damaging property. The county government issued a warrant for his arrest, but he has not been apprehended. Recently, the 15th branch of the Public Security Bureau was established in the district. Tang Yingchuan believed that the opportunity had come and went to the Yuqi Town branch on the evening of the 5th with his son Amao to report and request the arrest. Huang Sheng, the head of the branch, sent six policemen with guns and Tang and others to make the arrest. When they arrived at the village, it was about 3 a.m. In a rush, they mistakenly knocked on the door of Hu Xiaofa, who lived next to Tang Fugen. After entering Hu's house, they realized the mistake and immediately withdrew. However, Hu's daughters Ayun and Afeng were both frightened and became ill, and the door panels were damaged. Although Hu negotiated with Tang Yingchuan and others at the time, there was no result. After the police withdrew from Hu's house, they opened the back door of Fugen's house and searched extensively, arresting Fugen and taking him to the bureau. Hu's father, Rui Fu, who was 67 years old, was terrified. Afterwards, he saw that the sundries in the room were discarded on the ground, and ten silver dollars and two thousand copper coins hidden in the empty rice bin and broken cotton quilt were also gone. Huang, the head of the branch, prepared a document on the morning of the 6th and sent police by motorboat to send Fugen to the County Public Security Bureau in the city for interrogation. Hu Xiaofa believes that Tang Yingchuan should not have led the police to damage the door of another person and scare the children, and is preparing to file a formal complaint.

Water Police Capture Suspect in Cuiqiao Robbery Case 153

The massive robbery case in Cuiqiao Town, Wuyi County, is being investigated by the water and land police to recover the stolen goods. Liu Zishu, the first squad leader of the 10th team of the water police stationed in Qishuyan, captured a suspected robber, Chen Rongsheng, near Bailong Temple, Hengxiao Bridge, on the afternoon of the 5th. He was taken to the team for preliminary interrogation and confessed that his uncle Duogou was indeed a bad person, and that he himself was a good person. Squad Leader Liu is interrogating him, as a secret report indicates that he is a robber involved in the Cuiqiao robbery case.

Changshu

Dispute Between Telephone Subscribers and Company Over Price Increase 155

In order to compensate for the losses caused by the installation of automatic switchboards, the telephone company recently notified all subscribers that the price for telephone lines in shops would increase by one yuan, and the price for telephone lines in households and organizations would increase by half a yuan. As a result, a dispute arose between the company and subscribers. The Construction Bureau and the First District Office mediated for many days without a resolution. The Subscribers Association held a meeting at the Chamber of Commerce at 4 p.m. on the 4th. Eighty-four companies signed in and discussed the matter for a long time. The chairman then put two proposals to a vote: (1) Implement the previous resolution to send a letter to the company, limiting the date for removing the machines to the 7th of this month. When removing the machines, the company should return the deposit of 30 yuan to the subscribers. (2) The Electric Appliance Subscribers Association will publish a declaration to clarify the right and wrong between the company and the subscribers to the outside world. Finally, ten more companies were added to assist the supervisory committee in negotiating with the company.

Bandit Leader Liu Anbang from Haimen Brought to Changzhou 156

On the 16th of last month, the water and land military police of this county crossed the river from Hupu to Da'an Port to suppress the sea bandits. The county police escorted the bandit Liu to Hupu, and on the day before yesterday, Cheng Chongli, the supervisor of the County Public Security Bureau, was ordered to go to Hupu to escort the bandit Liu to the city. On the morning of the 5th, the Public Security Bureau reported the case to the County Government for handling according to law.

Nine sections of the Nantong embankment along the Yangtze River have been breached by the river tide, and twenty-five large and small dikes have been breached, flooding more than 50,000 mu of farmland. It has been decided to use labor instead of relief to speed up the construction of the retreat banks to prevent the flood season.

It is heard that the companies have already suffered from floods this year, and the harvest is only 30-40%. The losses from the current banditry are even greater.

Record of Military Law Trial 161

The joint military police inspection station arrested ten people who were causing trouble outside the North Gate, including Cao Awu, Zhou Busheng, Zhu Shisheng, Yao Yucheng, Xiao Xianbiao, Zhu Ziming, Sun Zongyan, Tang Libin, Jiang Guoxiu, and Ye Desheng. It also arrested fourteen people who were causing trouble at Banqiao outside the South Gate, including Meng Yunfa, Liu Yan, Zhang ZhanKui, Li Xueyin, Xiang Yun, Xue Lifa, Wang Deqing, Zhang Liting, Li Songlin, Han Chunyao, Zheng Baode, Wu Fengqi, Qian Songlin, and Yuan Guanghai. The military police were heavily armed. After the trial, Cao Awu (from Shanghai, 25 years old) and Zhou Busheng (from Hunan, 22 years old) were identified as the instigators. The officers and the Public Security Bureau Chief testified that Cao Awu chased and beat the police inspection station squad leader and inspectors, and Wang Deng and other inspectors testified that he robbed guns and injured the squad leader in the traffic inn and fired shots along the way into the city. Yao Yucheng testified. The circumstances of the other ten or so people, including Xiao Xianbiao, were less serious and may be irrelevant. How to handle the matter has been telegraphed to the superiors for instructions.

Militia Injure People While Inspecting Ships 163

The day before yesterday, a ship loaded with lilies and ginger was imported from Liuxu Port. The militia fired a warning shot, and one bullet hit the shipowner's head, killing him instantly. The ship's wife, distraught by the unprovoked shooting of her husband, did not want to live and drowned herself in the river. Now, there is only a child left on the ship, crying all day long. The ship is drifting in the Xiaojia Dai River.

Jiaxing

Party-Government Joint Meeting Reduces Rice Price 174

Recently, the rice price in Jiaxing City has been more expensive than in neighboring counties. Although the new rice season has arrived, the retail price of rice still requires 17.6 yuan, which has caused complaints from the public. Therefore, the County Executive Committee held a joint Party-Government meeting on the 5th at the County Party Headquarters. At the same time, members of the Rice Price Evaluation Committee were invited to participate in a joint discussion on reducing the rice price. The following resolutions were made: (1) The prices of all types of rice will be reduced starting from the 6th. The on-site price for winter rice was set at 16.9 yuan per shi (unit of measure), with white pointed rice and white rice having the same price. Number one Saigon rice will be 16.5 yuan, small twisted rice 14.5 yuan, and large twisted rice 12 yuan. All rice shops were notified to comply and not engage in under-the-table deals. The county government will issue a public notice to inform the public. (2) The retail rice prices at Tiande and Zhang Xingsheng rice shops were higher than the prices set by the Evaluation Committee. It was decided that both the Party and government sides would send personnel to investigate. If confirmed, the rice merchants will be handed over to the Rice Industry Association to determine a disciplinary method, which will be enforced by the County Government.

Incident Involving Special Agents 182

Private Grain Transportation Resolved with Fine 183

The rice price in the urban area has fallen sharply in recent days, approaching 10 yuan. Poor households were rejoicing at the relief, but unexpectedly, the price suddenly increased by seven cents on the evening of the 2nd, which alarmed everyone. On the morning of the 3rd, the county party headquarters received a report that Che Fu Dan and Che Wen Gui, father and son from the Zhen Kang Rice Shop outside the east gate, were manipulating the rice price, monopolizing the market, and transporting rice out of the county in batches. After investigation, it was confirmed that a boat loaded with rice was being transported to Tang Pu, Shao Xing. The police officers were dispatched to Wupo Ling and intercepted the boat. Wu Shao Qi and two other rice merchants on the boat went ashore to hide. The seized rice amounted to twenty-two bags, each containing one shi and six dou, totaling thirty-five shi, worth 350 yuan. The department convened a meeting with party and government officials and business representatives. As a result, considering their ignorance, they were leniently dealt with and ordered the Zhen Kang Rice Shop to pay a fine of 70 yuan (50 yuan to compensate for the grain consumption deficit in the first district and 20 yuan to reward the informant). They also required a guarantee that they would not privately transport grain again. The seized cargo ship was returned. However, the local people were still dissatisfied and planned to jointly request strict legal action to warn unscrupulous merchants.

Letter Received

Letter from Cheng Bingyao 184

I recently read in the "Important News" section of your newspaper on July 4th about the joint attack by the Fujian Sea and Land Army on Lu's troops. At the end, it mentioned that the defense of Shaowu and Jianou and other areas in the rear was undertaken by the two regiments of Huang Qingcai and Cheng Bingyao, implying that Lu Xingrong did not trust these two regiments from Minqing. After reading this, I was very surprised. Cheng Bingyao's ancestral home is Gutian. Since resigning from the position of regimental commander in the summer of the 17th year, I have been dedicated to education. Last summer, I returned to Gutian and was appointed as the director of the Guping Branch Road Engineering Office by the Fujian Construction Department last winter. Since then, I have only been involved in road planning and have not been involved in other affairs. The report in your newspaper must be based on rumors and is inaccurate. I am writing this special letter to request an immediate correction. Sincerely, Cheng Bingyao, July 20, Year 19

Local News

Insufficient Rice Supply 185

Difficult to Export

Recently, the Municipal Government of this city received letters from the Qingdao Municipal Government requesting permission to export rice. However, considering that the population of this city is increasing year by year and the food supply depends entirely on Su rice, which is already insufficient, it is difficult to export. A letter was sent to Qingdao City yesterday stating: We acknowledge the receipt of your government's official letters No. 3750 and No. 4025, stating that according to the Qingdao General Chamber of Commerce, Hongshengxiang Company intends to purchase white rice in Shanghai to supply the people of Qingdao, temporarily limited to 1,000 dan per month, and requests a special permit for a one-year trial period. The Social Affairs Bureau also requested the transfer of rice to Qingdao to relieve the people's food shortage and requested permission to export and issue a passport, allowing 2,000 bags of rice to be transported each month. After investigation, this city is not a rice-producing area, and the population is increasing year by year. The food supply depends almost entirely on Su rice, and there is no surplus for export. Therefore, it is difficult to handle the Japonica rice. However, foreign rice and Ke Xian rice can be re-exported. Historically, various provinces and cities have come to Shanghai to purchase foreign rice. The rice merchants first submit the rice amount purchased to the provincial and municipal governments for approval and issuance of passports, which are then taken to the Social Affairs Bureau of this city for verification before release. Therefore, we are responding to your letter and requesting that you inform us accordingly. This is addressed to the Qingdao Municipal Government.

The Jianghai Customs Supervisory Office of this city received an order from the Ministry of Finance to strictly prohibit the export of rice, grain, and wheat flour to northern ports to avoid causing further food panic. Japanese Destroyer Squadron Arrived in Shanghai Yesterday 188

Three Ships - Momo, Yanagi, and Kashi

Hinoki to Enter Port This Morning

Fully Prepared for Combat

The Japanese Ministry of Navy, citing the pretext of banditry on the Yangtze River to protect Japanese residents, suddenly ordered the four ships of the Sasebo 24th Destroyer Squadron, Momo, Yanagi, Kashi, and Hinoki, to sail to China for defense on the day before yesterday. Three ships, Momo, Kashi, and Yanagi, arrived successively at 5:30 PM yesterday. After entering the port, they were anchored at the Pudong naval buoys and the Whampoo Wharf. The Hinoki will enter port this morning (the 7th). In addition to the original officers and soldiers, each warship carries more than 300 specially selected naval landing troops. In addition to one captain on each ship, Yanagihara was also appointed as the commander to lead the ships. The warships are all painted fish white, and the equipment, food, and coal are abundant, fully prepared for combat emergencies. They will sail to various ports on the Yangtze River as soon as the second order is issued. The above warships have all sailed on the Yangtze River during the last large-scale Japanese warship visit to China, so they are very familiar with the Yangtze River voyage. Currently, Changsha has been recovered, and the Hunan-Hubei bandits and communists have been suppressed by the central government. It is reported that all levels of party headquarters and public organizations are protesting this alarming action by the Japanese and requesting the central government to ban it.

Will Be Ordered to Sail to the Yangtze River

The US Naval Commander's Office in China issued an order yesterday that all officers and soldiers on warships stationed in Shanghai are not allowed to leave the ship and are waiting for orders to depart. Zhu Maocheng Returned to China the Day Before Yesterday 191

Talking About the Mission to Europe

Mr. Zhu Maocheng, the government representative of our country to the 14th International Labor Conference, returned to Shanghai on the Fengtian Maru on the 5th. Yesterday, he told the Guowen News Agency reporters about the details of the conference, which have been mostly covered in the previous Geneva communications. In addition to attending the International Labor Conference, Zhu left Shanghai on April 29th this year to lead the delegation of our country to the Second World Power Conference in Berlin. He also went to Liège, Belgium to participate in the World Expo and attended the International Labor Holiday Conference there. He delivered a speech at the conference on behalf of various countries, which attracted the attention of the Belgians. Before returning to China, Zhu received a telegram from the Ministry of Industry and Commerce to return to Geneva to attend the "International Conference on Budget Law and Scientific Management." The conference opened on July 10th and lasted for three days. More than 200 experts in industry and commerce from various countries attended the conference and discussed in detail various issues in scientific management, which were very important. This type of conference is a new era in the development of the world economy. After the conference, Zhu briefly stayed in Germany for a few days, visiting German sugar factories, shipyards, and other industries, and then took the Eurasian through train via Siberia to return to China.

Japanese Financial Officer Dismissed and Transferred 192

Kozumori Taro Returns to China Tomorrow

Kozumori Taro, the financial officer of the Japanese Embassy in China, has been in office for a long time. Yesterday, he suddenly received a telegram from the Ministry of Finance of the Japanese government stating that the post of financial officer in China was being abolished and the position of financial officer was being cancelled due to the implementation of austerity policies and the reduction of government expenses. The original financial officer Kozumori Taro was transferred to the position of director of the Industrial Bank of Japan. After receiving the order, Financial Officer Kozumori started the closing procedures yesterday and is scheduled to return to China on a ship tomorrow (the 8th) to report for duty. It is reported that the abolition of the financial officer's office can save tens of thousands of yuan in expenses each year. In addition, matters relating to Sino-Japanese loans, customs duties, and finance will be handled directly by the Japanese Embassy.

Previous Reports About Minting New National Currency 193

New Model Arrived

According to financial circles, the government recently ordered a new national currency model from a certain country, which has been manufactured and submitted to the Ministry of Finance for appraisal. It is said that the style is similar to the ordinary national currency circulating in the market, with the Prime Minister's portrait on the front and a pattern similar to the stamp pattern on the back, with a sailboat and the words "National Currency of the Republic of China," but without any foreign characters. This coin model has been stored by the Beijing Mint and will be decided whether to implement a virtual gold standard after the Ministry of Finance and the Ministry of Industry and Commerce have discussed it. If the virtual gold standard cannot be implemented, then this new model national currency will be ordered by the mint to cast coins, which can be issued in the shortest period of time. If the virtual gold standard is implemented, then another type of coin model will be required.

Ministry Order to Stop Zhejiang Province from Re-levying Cloth Donations 194

Silk and Mercerized Cotton Weaving Industry Can Rest Assured

The Shanghai Chamber of Commerce replied to the Shanghai Silk and Mercerized Cotton Weaving Industry Association yesterday, stating: We acknowledge the receipt of your letter dated July 21st, stating that the cotton weaving business is declining day by day and proposing three relief measures for separate review and handling. Items two and three have been submitted to the Municipal Social Affairs Bureau for forwarding and have not yet been replied. Item one, the Yongjia Unified Donation Bureau's levy of cloth donations, has been telegraphed to the Ministry of Finance and the Zhejiang Provincial Government to comply with the regulations. We received a telegram from the Ministry of Finance Fu Zi No. 4663 on August 5th, stating that we have carefully reviewed the telegraph stating that Chinese imitation cotton fabrics, if registered with the Ministry of Industry and Commerce's trademark registration company and approved by the Ministry to pay taxes on machine-made Western-style goods, have obtained certificates for paying the correct and additional taxes at the first customs office for export and have no intention of obscuring or confusing the matter. They are exempt from paying all other donations when sold in the mainland. The Ministry previously received a report from the Zhejiang Yongjia Silk and Cloth Industry Association requesting the cessation of the re-levy of cloth donations in Zhejiang. An order has been issued to the Zhejiang Department of Finance for investigation and handling. We are now telegraphing the details to you to check and inform us. This is addressed to the Shanghai Silk and Mercerized Cotton Weaving Industry Association.

Postal Parcel Tax Abolition is Scheduled 195

Ministry of Finance Replies to City Chamber of Commerce by Telegram

The Shanghai Chamber of Commerce yesterday sent separate letters to the Shanghai Postal Workers' Union, Postal Workers' Union, and Silk and Satin Industry Association's Rectification Committee, stating: We acknowledge that relevant industry groups have successively requested the abolition of the postal parcel tax. We have now received a telegram from the Ministry of Finance No. 4668 stating that the abolition of the Likin has been ordered and scheduled to be implemented. The postal parcel tax is a type of Likin and has been planned to be abolished at the scheduled time. We are informing you separately by recording the telegram and requesting that you check accordingly.

Transportation Association Submits a Document to the City Chamber of Commerce 196

Request to Cancel Increased Deposit Payment

The Shanghai Jinghu Road Transportation Association submitted a document to the City Chamber of Commerce yesterday, stating: We received a letter from the Pukou Transportation Association on July 25th, which received a telegram from the Pukou Stationmaster stating that the Transportation Bureau had transferred it to all transporting merchants, who have all seen that the bureau had previously amended the regulations on vehicle requests by merchants due to the fact that merchants along the line often set up shops for speculation and requested vehicles to control freight transport. The amount of security deposit to be paid was stipulated according to the starting station, etc., and was promulgated and implemented in April of the tenth year. However, since the implementation of the regulations, the amount of the security deposit was too low, resulting in merchants still being mixed and uneven. Whenever empty cars arrive at the station, there are many people requesting them. For example, the Bengbu station has more than 70 companies vying for vehicles. At this time of frequent military transportation, the demand exceeds the supply. Even after the military situation is settled, it will still be difficult to cope with it. In order to strictly prevent control, false reports, and to reorganize freight transportation, the Beijiang Grade A Pukou and other four stations will increase by 2,000 yuan per station, the Grade B Chu Dan and other eleven stations will increase by 1,000 yuan per station, and the Grade C Wuyi and other seventeen stations will increase by 500 yuan per station. The increased funds will be paid in full before September 10th. The Bureau will give merchants who increase the payment of this deposit within the time limit the right to allocate vehicles first. Those who do not comply with the payment will not enjoy the right to allocate vehicles in advance. We are informing you and requesting that you check and handle the matter and not wait and see and delay your own affairs. Our association has held a meeting to discuss the matter. All members agreed that the industry has been repeatedly affected by military affairs, and the supply of Jinpu vehicles for military use has caused the companies to lose money. In the previous year, they complied with the payment of 1 million yuan in public bonds for purchasing cars, and in the previous year, they increased the payment of a total of 500,000 yuan in security deposits for requesting cars. The purchase and requisition of cars are closely related, so they had to comply with the order to pay. Until now, the interest that should be paid is still being deferred. Most of the money paid by the companies comes from loans. The Bureau does not care for them and limits the time to increase the deposit, and its name is reorganization, and the time limit for increasing the payment is given the right to allocate vehicles in advance. In other words, the security deposit paid in the previous year is equal to a waste. Moreover, recently there is not only no whole car available for allocation, but even small-volume goods are piled up in Pukou, and the losses of the transporters cannot be overstated. Even the car requisition security deposit paid in the previous year has not benefited the companies. Continuing to persevere in the future is no less than putting all transporters to death. In addition to the companies jointly requesting the Pukou Nanning Transportation Industry Association to request the Ministry of Railways to order the Jinpu Railway Bureau to cancel the increased deposit payment and to reorganize the vehicles to deal with freight transportation to alleviate commercial difficulties, and to check the news report on July 29th in which the Ministry of Industry and Commerce proposed a transportation facilitation program with a total of eight points. The fourth point of the eight points, "Strictly prohibit extractions of transportation fees," coincides with the clause in the Jinpu Railway Bureau's order to increase the deposit payment. The opinions of the Ministry of Railways have been submitted to the National Government for review, and the State Council has decided to transfer them to the administrative authorities to take responsibility for handling the matter. Our association has reported the situation to each company and hereby requests your association to send a telegram to the Ministry of Railways to give preferential treatment to the transporters, to quickly order the Jinpu Bureau to cancel the increased deposit payment, to reorganize the vehicles, to dredge the freight transport, and to ask the Ministry to expedite the apportionment of the interest from the car requisition security deposit and the car purchase public bond interest from the previous year to maintain credit and alleviate commercial difficulties.

Another Smuggling of Gold Bars Discovered on Japanese Ship 197

Found on the Ikoma Maru

A Total of More Than 40 Bars

Since the Customs issued a ban on the export of gold, the smuggling of gold bars from Shanghai to Japan has been common. The Jianghai Customs has stepped up inspection efforts and is even stricter in inspecting ships going to Japan. The Ikoma Maru of the Japanese Post Office in this port, which was loading cargo in Shanghai and scheduled to export to Osaka and Kobe yesterday morning, had customs inspectors on board twice to inspect the ship. More than 40 smuggled gold bars were found, worth more than 40,000 taels of silver. The smuggler who smuggled the gold bars was arrested by the crew members for prosecution.

French Merchant Water and Electricity Workers' Strike - Yesterday's News 200

Negotiations with the Factory Yesterday Were Unsuccessful

Negotiation Situation 201

The strike by French merchant water and electricity workers has dragged on for nearly two months. Although the authorities have intervened several times, no results have been achieved. Recently, the French Consul has been responsible for mediation, but the extent of the mediation and the date of the completion of the resolution are still unknown. Workers believe that although this prolonged strike is a struggle against imperialism, some sacrifices are unavoidable, but prolonged delays are not a long-term solution. The mediators find the proceedings difficult and unusually difficult. Therefore, in the previous general meeting, it was unanimously decided to elect eight representatives to go to the factory yesterday morning to ask the manager, M. Menssolon, about the situation. In the morning, M. Menssolon was unable to meet with them due to other important matters. They made an appointment to go at 3:00 PM. The representatives of the union included two people from the Chinese staff department, two people from the writing department, two people from the transportation department, and two people from the mechanical department. They went to the meeting as scheduled at 3:00 PM and were received by M. Menssolon. The representatives then asked M. Menssolon about the attitude he would take regarding the matter based on the opinions of the general meeting. M. Menssolon said that the union had requested intervention from the Central Government and could ask the Central Government about the attitude. He was very tough and said that he could not accept the opinions of the representatives at all. The representatives then told the manager that no matter how the Central Government mediated or how the French Consul proceeded, they must give a satisfactory answer within two days before leaving. When the two sides were in contact, the factory was heavily guarded.

Union Attitude 202

The union had originally planned to convene a general meeting of all employees at the Public Sports Field after negotiating with the manager yesterday, but the negotiation time was changed to 3:00 PM, so the meeting was temporarily cancelled and changed to a partial meeting at the union at 5:00 PM. After the negotiations broke down, the workers were extremely angry and unanimously stated that they would not stop until they reached their goal. Chen Pu Ai was dispatched to the Support Association to report the situation and decided on three cases: (1) The foreman of the paint workshop, Chen, was accused of disrupting strike discipline and was handed over to the interrogation section for investigation by the disciplinary team. (2) Request the Municipal Party Department to resolve the labor dispute as soon as possible. (3) Anyone who disrupts the union will be investigated by union members and dealt with forcefully.

Supporting Meeting 203

Because this labor dispute has been prolonged, the supporting committee convened a special meeting at the Municipal Party Headquarters, third floor, yesterday at 1 p.m. More than three hundred representatives from various labor unions in the city attended. Hu Shouqi, Zhang Yaoming, and Chen Peide were elected as the presidium, with Ye Yunping as the recorder. After the ritual greetings, the chairman reported on the situation of support. Subsequently, Xu A'mei, a representative from the French Water and Electricity Workers' Union, reported on the course of the recent strike and the facts of the "July 21st Tragedy." She also made a definite statement regarding the recent arrest of two members of the union's executive committee, Wang A'gen and Su Jiliang. Li Shizeng, a member of the Central Committee, originally planned to attend the meeting to report, but was prevented by an unforeseen circumstance. The assembly sent representatives to his residence to make contact. Then the assembly discussed the proposals: (1) To organize a city-wide labor support committee to issue a strong declaration regarding the "July 21st Tragedy." Twenty-one representatives from the supporting committee groups were elected on the spot, including Yu Yaoqiu from the Taikang Food Workers' Union, Zhang Yaoming from the Nanhua Reception Workers' Union, Zhang Linhua from the Xiang Sheng Iron Factory Workers' Union, Ye Gonglun from the Shanghai-Ningbo Steamboat Crew Union, Gu Yongquan from the Mercerizing and Dyeing Workers' Union, Chen Peide from the British-American Tobacco Factory Workers' Union, Wang Wenhua from the Commercial Workers Union, Xu Shaochuan from the Southern Goods Workers Union, Weng Ruifu from the Sauce Industry Workers Union, Li Yongxiang from the Zhabei Water and Electricity Workers Union, Ge Yunting from the Cotton Weaving Workers Union, Zhu Shaoyun from the Dyeing Industry Workers Union, Hu Shouqi from the Calligraphy and Fan Workers Union, Fan Pusheng from the Commercial Workers Union, Zhao Zhenhui from the Pharmaceutical Industry Workers Union, Mei Guozhen from the Newspaper Delivery Workers Union, He Che from the Chinese and Foreign Cloth Industry Workers Union, Lu Jingshi from the Postal Workers Union, Zhou Xuexiang from the Huacheng Tobacco Workers Union, Tang Junsheng from the Chinese Water and Electricity Workers Union, and Long Peiyun from the Qiuxin Shipyard Workers Union. The presidium convened a temporary meeting with the above representatives to discuss and decide to issue a declaration in the name of the committee, to be drafted by Cai Xiaohe. (2) Yu Yaoqiu proposed sending letters to the Songhu Garrison Headquarters and the Municipal Public Security Bureau, requesting guarantees against the arrest of French Water and Electricity workers. It was resolved to submit the request to the Party Headquarters for transmission. (3) It was resolved that the assembly would send three representatives to inquire about the mediation situation from Li Shizeng, a member of the Central Committee, together with representatives from the French Water and Electricity Workers Union. Gu Yongquan, Lu Jingshi, and Hu Shouqi were immediately elected to go. (4) It was resolved to assist the French Electric Company Workers Union with economic problems. In addition to the already issued order that each worker donate one jiao, further assistance would be provided by each labor union as much as possible. All the above resolutions were passed. Chen Puwen, who was in contact with the factory, also arrived and immediately reported on the progress. All the representatives were indignant. Xia Menghuan, a representative from the Japanese-Chinese Workers Union, also reported on the Japanese factory's abuse of workers and the recent labor disputes. It was also resolved to provide unanimous assistance and issue a declaration in the name of the assembly to provide support. The meeting was adjourned after guidance from representatives of the Municipal Department.

Chen Junyi, a standing committee member of the Municipal People's Training Association, attended the People’s Training Meeting upon invitation by Central Committee member Dai Jitao. He has now returned to Shanghai after completing his assignment. It is said that in addition to discussing national training matters, the French business labor dispute was also brought up for discussion. Yangtze River Shipping News

[P Upstream Cargo Shipment

In the past two weeks, tens of thousands of pieces of cargo destined for Hunan that were blocked and returned to Hankou. Even goods from Yichang could not be shipped. The unloading of upstream cargo was almost completely blocked. Yesterday, a Shanghai-based steamship company received a telegram from Hankou stating that the Communist bandits in Changsha had been defeated by the Central Army and that navigation on the Hunan-Hubei waterway had resumed. The steamship's blocked cargo had already departed from Hankou for Changsha, and Yichang was resuming normal loading and unloading. This is the first batch of goods from Hunan to resume transportation.

Chinese Merchants Request Ships 206

Chinese shipping merchants in Yichang telegraphed various steamship companies in Shanghai yesterday, stating that the Chinese steamships on the upper reaches of the Yangtze River have been suspended for a long time, and Chinese shipping has been completely taken over by foreign steamships. Not only have Chinese shipping merchants suffered huge losses, but they are also unable to maintain the current situation. Now that transportation is gradually decreasing, they request that Shanghai shipping merchants consult with the Communications Department to release three or four steamships to resume routes to Yichang, Shashi, and Chongqing in order to relieve the livelihoods of the shipping industries in the upper reaches of the Yangtze River.

Since Cai Pei took office as the acting director of the China Merchants Steam Navigation Company, he has continued to implement the old system in the bureau's affairs. Assisting in the Rescue of the Accident Ship and Recording

Guangli Can Escape Danger 208

The China Merchants Steam Navigation Company's Guangli steamship ran aground on Gelan Island below the Parrot Island in the upper reaches of Hankou. Repeated attempts to tow it have been unsuccessful. The crew and sailors have all left the ship and transferred to Shanghai. The Wuhan authorities have been requested to send troops to protect it. Since it ran aground, it has been two weeks. Due to the shallow water and difficulty in towing, they have been waiting for the tide to rise. Yesterday, they received a telegram from the steamship stating that the water level on Gelan Island has risen by more than a foot. The Hankou branch was requested to send the Lijia steamship to tow it. It is hoped that it can be pulled out of the shallow water today and towed to Shanghai for major repairs.

[P Flying Tiger Salvaged Again

The Sanbei's Flying Tiger steamship was sunk by a warship on the Hankou Jiang'an River on February 22nd. The bureau immediately entrusted the Shanghai Rongchang Development Company to salvage it. It was not easy to rescue it immediately. On the one hand, it requested the headquarters to recognize the loss for compensation. This matter has been going on for more than five months. Now it is heard that the headquarters has agreed to酌认赔款 [Consider Approving Compensation], and the salvage project has gradually become effective recently, and it is hoped that it can be rescued. Therefore, work is continuing in these days.

Haimen County Closes All Ports 209

To Prevent Bandit Troubles and Clear Bandit Sources

The Shipping Association Notifies Fellow Traders

The Shipping Association of this port sent a letter to Jufeng, Xinlong, Dada, Ping'an, Daxing, and other companies yesterday, stating: "We hereby inform you that we have received a document from the Haimen County Chamber of Commerce, sealed and sent by the Haimen County Government, regarding the closure of all ports to prevent bandit troubles. We are now enclosing a copy of this document for your reference and compliance." Attached is Haimen County Government Order No. 445, which states: "In order to comply with the order, this government's 48th County Administration Conference discussed Public Security Bureau Chief Hao Zhiying's proposal. The coastal area of Hai County is adjacent to the river, and the ports are scattered. Bandits come and go frequently, and smuggled goods such as firearms are often brought into the country, endangering public security. In the past, it was proposed at the County Administration Conference to close the ports, which is indeed an important way to eliminate troubles. However, due to the obstruction of transportation, it was not possible to close all of them. Two methods are proposed: (1) Lingdian Port, Qinglong Port, Daxin Port, Songji Port, and Niuhong Port are important transportation ports and should not be closed. It is proposed that the police stationed at various public security sub-bureaus and outposts should strictly inspect them, and the county government should order the district chiefs of each district to instruct the township chiefs along the port and notify the water police to cooperate in strict patrols. (2) Material closure of ports with small ports, sparse ships, and insufficient police patrols, such as Yuehe Port, Lao Ji Port, Yueya Port, Taiping Port, Jiepai Port, and other small ports, will be the responsibility of the public security sub-bureaus and outposts to close with various materials. The required materials will be purchased by the Property Division. Whether the above two methods are applicable, such as Da'an Port, which is wide and large, but is a gathering place for bandits, has already been included in the closure list. However, there is a customs office at that place. If the port is closed, will it affect the national tax revenue? All should be submitted for discussion." It was resolved: "(1) Do not close each port, and order them to be handled separately according to the case. (2) The county government should issue a notice prohibiting ships from passing through the ports that should be closed, and order the district offices to instruct the township chiefs of each port to send two secret agents to each port to inspect at any time. If any ships are found entering or leaving, report them immediately to the nearest public security bureau or outpost for detention, and give preferential rewards." In addition to issuing notices and orders separately, it is hereby ordered that the association comply and notify all ship owners that all ports previously prohibited from closing should temporarily suspend berthing in order to clear bandit sources. If anyone dares to disobey, they will be heavily fined without leniency. This order is urgent."

Urgent Progress in Implementing the Wusong Dredging Project 210

Meeting to be Held to Discuss Fundraising Methods

The lower reaches of the Wusong River are silted up with mud and sand, and the river water is shallow, causing many obstructions to ships traveling back and forth. The Municipal Government of this city and various water conservancy agencies once convened a meeting to prepare for dredging, but the project was so large and fundraising so difficult that no progress was made. It is now learned that the Construction Committee believes that if the Wusong River's silted waterway is not dredged as soon as possible, the sand and mud will inevitably become more and more silted, and water transportation will be more and more affected. Therefore, it has specially formulated a plan for dredging the Wusong River, and after review, it has been completed. Yesterday, the Municipal Finance Bureau, the Municipal Chamber of Commerce, the Wusong Water Conservancy Association, the Shanghai Dredging Bureau, and other agencies of this city received letters from the Construction Committee requesting that each agency propose fundraising methods and send them to the committee in order to hold a meeting on a scheduled basis to discuss. Once the fundraising methods are properly discussed and finalized, the dredging of the Wusong River will begin.

Trade Associations Must Complete Reorganization Within a Time Limit 212

The Municipal Chamber of Commerce Notifies All Industries to Comply

The Shanghai Municipal Chamber of Commerce issued a notice to all trade associations yesterday, stating: "We hereby inform you that we have received Order No. 2635 from the Shanghai Municipal Bureau of Social Affairs on August 1, which was issued by the Municipal Government, which in turn was issued by the Executive Yuan, which in turn was issued by the Central Executive Committee's Letter No. 10259, forwarding three measures for the reorganization of merchant groups in various places, ordering compliance. Articles 1, 2, and 3 of these measures are different from the situation in this city and will not be described in detail. All Article 1 states that the reorganization of merchant groups in Zhejiang, Guangzhou, Shanghai, and other provinces and cities that have been approved by the central merchant group guidance and reorganization agencies should be completed within the time limit approved by the National Government in accordance with the approved laws and procedures. We have forwarded the order to the association. The Law on Industrial and Commercial Trade Associations was promulgated by the National Government on August 17, 1929. According to Article 14 of this law, trade associations established in accordance with this law should be reorganized in accordance with this law within one year after the implementation of this law. Therefore, all trade associations in this city should complete their reorganization by August 16 of this year. Before receiving the order, we hereby issue a notice urging all trade associations to formally complete their reorganization within the statutory time limit and not to delay any further. This is of utmost importance."

The Municipal Chamber of Commerce Requests That Soldiers Be Ordered to Vacate the Association's Premises 213

The Shanghai Municipal Chamber of Commerce sent a letter to the Songhu Garrison Headquarters yesterday, stating: "We hereby inform you that the premises of the Shanghai Steel and Tin Trade Association (formerly the Steel and Tin Trade Guild) have been occupied by soldiers of the 28th Regiment of the 14th Brigade of the 5th Division. Reorganization and restructuring are impossible, and the association's affairs are difficult to handle. In April of this year, the former Chamber of Commerce reported the situation and requested evacuation. It was approved and forwarded to the regiment to find another location. The association was notified when a location was found. Now, the Reorganization Committee of the Trade Association has sent a letter stating that the Trade Association has received orders from the ministry to complete the reorganization according to law within a time limit, but the association's premises are still occupied by soldiers, and there is no place to hold meetings, so it cannot proceed. It was previously indicated that the premises of each trade association and the recruitment of soldiers by labor unions should not be arbitrarily occupied, and it has been resolved by the representatives of the members to send letters to the respective orders. It is now the association's premises, and the aforementioned soldiers have not yet moved out. We hereby report again, hoping that you will earnestly forward the request for evacuation as soon as possible so that the reorganization can be completed as soon as possible." After investigation, the Law on Industrial and Commercial Trade Associations was promulgated on August 17, 1929. According to Article 14 of this law, trade associations established in accordance with this law should be reorganized within one year after the implementation of this law. Now that the deadline is approaching, the Municipal Bureau of Social Affairs has repeatedly forwarded orders from the ministry to reorganize according to the time limit and forward them for compliance. The Trade Association cannot proceed with the reorganization due to the occupation of the association's premises. It is impossible to comply with the ministry's order to reorganize according to the time limit, and it is impossible to proceed with the association's affairs and maintain the merchants' interests. Furthermore, it is forbidden to recruit soldiers and others to occupy the premises of the Trade Association without permission. The Gui Ministry has previously sent a letter ordering compliance. Now, the soldiers of the regiment have been occupying the premises for a long time and have not moved out, which is inconsistent with the Gui Ministry's intention to order compliance. We hereby report the situation and request that you examine and approve it and quickly forward the order to the regiment's soldiers to evacuate by a certain date in order to maintain sovereignty and sincerity. This is addressed to the Songhu Garrison Headquarters.

Hunan Fellow Villagers Appeal for Hunan Affairs 214

The Shanghai Hunan Fellow Villagers Association sent a telegram to the Central News Agency, forwarding it to all levels of Party Headquarters, all military and political leaders, all mass organizations, and all compatriots throughout the country: "Recently, Communist bandits have sprung up in the three provinces of Hunan, Hubei, and Jiangxi. Bandit leader Peng Dehuai gathered more than 10,000 people and captured Changsha on the night of July 27. The provincial government, the provincial Party Headquarters, various agencies, and all stores, banks, customs offices, public and private schools, and civilian houses in the city were all looted and then burned. The flames soared into the sky and have not stopped for days. The residents of the city, supporting the old and leading the young, fled in droves, but only 10,000 people escaped. The remaining 300,000 citizens, caught off guard and unable to escape, were killed in countless numbers. Corpses littered the ground, and blood flowed like a river. The tragedy is unprecedented. Changsha has not yet been recovered (note: Changsha was recovered on the 5th), and rumors are rife in Nanxun and Wuhan, causing panic. If this bandit force is not quickly suppressed, a red disaster will inevitably spread and poison the entire country. We hope that all our compatriots will rise up together to exterminate this giant bandit and appeal to the authorities to immediately send elite troops to suppress them in order to save the people of Hunan and ensure national security. We weep and present our urgent request, awaiting orders. All the fellow villagers in Shanghai bow down in support."

It was decided to temporarily留 [Retain] the administrative expenses of the district offices in July, August, and September. After the Shanghai Municipal Government's subsidy funds are resolved and the county government's administrative subsidies are received, the borrowed and墊 [Advanced] amounts will be returned as they are. Jishenghui Relief for Ninghai Disaster 221

According to Sun Jinyin Tingdong, director of the Ninghai 工振 [Labor Relief] Department of the China Jishenghui, in a telegram from Ninghai, "I arrived in Ninghai last night to handle the 工 [Labor]. I walked three or four li on muddy roads, which was difficult to travel. When I arrived at the second branch, I was surprised to find that most of the people in the area were in the sea. It was learned that on the night of the day before last month, due to continuous heavy rains, a torrential flood suddenly broke out like a landslide, turning the entire area into a泽国 [Waterlogged Land]. From Baiqiao, 10 li east of the county, to Yuejing in the far east, from Dongyu, 20 li south of the county, to Huayu Jiankangtang in the far south, and from Qiaotouhu, 30 li north of the county, to Xiashan Jiajueke in the far north, each line stretches for hundreds of li or seventy or eighty li. There are no less than thousands of海 [Sea] ports. According to statistics, the塘田 [Pond Fields] reach more than one million mu, all of which have been收掇 [Cleared up] by 波臣 [God of Waves]. The survivors are less than two or three out of ten. Among the works repaired by the association, 72塘 [Ponds] inside and outside the Bainei of Zhongdu, Xiadu, and Youdu were breached by Qingye, causing damage to about 13,000 mu of rice fields and affecting more than 5,000 people whose livelihoods have been cut off. How can we relieve them in the long term? The 工振 [Labor Relief] for repairing the堤塘 [Dikes] in the area proposed by the association previously requires a three-fold increase in the estimated amount based on the current缺口线 [Gap Line] of more than one hundred places to complete the work. In addition to rushing to plug the breach to protect 민망 [Peoples Houses] and 민망 [Peoples Lives], it is necessary to find ways to increase relief money in order to save people and免填沟壑 [Avoid Filling Gullies]. "In addition, the county magistrate Tang Tiansen and the villagers of the 해 [Sea] villages in the east, south, and north three towns, and the village chiefs of Gudu and Zhongdu, sent telegrams to the same effect. The association found that the association's 工振 [Labor Relief] in Ninghai was already led by the previous Ninghai relief director, Sun Jinyin Ting, and Zhenyou Li Yunmen Xie Yu, who rushed to repair the堤塘 [Dikes] to prevent floods. Now, the堤塘 [Dikes] have been breached by sudden floods. According to the original budget, it is impossible to solve the problem without raising three times the amount. The association's public discussion of the difficulty of raising funds has reached the extreme, and there is only hope to do its best to fulfill its wishes. However, the sudden disaster cannot be saved by the original sole force. It is hoped that the compatriots in Zhejiang and the domestic charitable organizations will support and assist.

The Question of Lawyers' Uniforms Along the Border 222

Differences between white silk and treasury silver

Lawyer Yao Wenshou put forward his opinions on the lawyers' uniforms to the Shanghai Lawyers Association, saying that it is not appropriate to replace white silk with treasury silver (commonly known as back-pattern silver) for the borders of lawyers' uniforms. According to the principle that lawyers should be clean, selfless, and not hold selfish interests first when performing their duties, the central government promulgated that the collars and edges of lawyers' uniforms should be made of white silk to show that lawyers are clean and flawless, which is a sign of respect for character and encouragement of integrity. Now, the association previously proposed to replace it with treasury silver, which, from a superficial point of view, seems to conform to the colors promulgated by the central government. However, it is my opinion that treasury silver, although it is also silk, inevitably contains gold and silver colors and cannot be considered pure white. Therefore, although it is magnificent, it does not conform to the original purpose. Moreover, it is said that lawyers' uniforms in the courts of Jiangsu and Zhejiang provinces do not use treasury silver, and Shanghai is the only region that is unique, which may not be appropriate. Furthermore, the price difference between white silk and treasury silver is huge, and it is uneconomical to use it for edges. Therefore, I have put forward my opinions for public decision.

A Girl Killed by a Car 224

Shen Ke'er, a driver from Haimen of Yinghai Heji Automobile Company at 582 Zhonghua Road, Xiaonanmen, drove a truck with municipal government registration number 4313 to Zhabei on the afternoon of the day before yesterday at seven o'clock. On the way, when passing near Tanjiachiao and Pengpu New Bridge, Zhang Zhufa, a resident of Guanyintang No. 33, leading his eight-year-old adopted daughter Ge Lexiu, was walking slowly on the road. Since the sun had set and the sky was dark, he could not辨物 [Distinguish things]. Shen's car was driving very fast, and he did not see anyone at first. When he noticed, it was too late to brake, and he knocked down the girl Ge Lexiu,碾伤 [Crushing Injury] her head and neck, etc., with blood everywhere. She was killed on the spot. Seeing that he had caused the accident, Shen intended to escape at full speed, but he was鸣笛 [Sounded the Whistle] and chased by a passerby Zhang Jinshan. He was eventually arrested by members of the first 防所 [Defense Department] of the second guard team at the location, and together with the corpse, his father Zhang Zhufa, and witness Zhang Jinshan, he was sent to the fourth district總署 [Headquarters]. After interrogation by署长 [Director] Jin, he submitted the documents to the judicial section for核辦 [Review and Handling] yesterday.

A Motorist Drives Illegally 225

A Primary School Student Dies Tragically

Wu Zhou's son, Wu Genquan, nine years old, from No. 3 Huasheng Lane, Huasheng Road, Zhabei, was returning home from school for lunch on the day before yesterday, walking on the south side of the road. The motorist Wang A'gen drove illegally on the north side of the road, but instead of driving on the north side where he should have been, he drove on the south side. As a result, Wu Genquan suffered无妄之灾 [Unexpected Disaster] and was knocked down and碾毙 [Rolled to death]. Subsequently, the Fourth District Police Department arrested and detained Wang A'gen. Wang's family negotiated with Wu Zhou's family not to pursue the matter and paid a sum of money for damages. The woman requested not to pursue the matter, but the police department refused. They were transferred to the local court for interrogation and ordered the eleventh map保 [Guarantor] Shen Xiaohe to submit a report to the court for驗 [Inspection].

Lok Ming-tak Seeks Relatives and Attempts Suicide by Drowning 226

Fortunately Rescued by a Boatman

Lok Ming-tak, a 22-year-old from Ningbo, had been living in Hankou as a clerk at a customs brokerage. Recently, Lok's parents brought his 7-year-old younger sister to Shanghai. His father intended to find a proper job but had been lodging with relatives for several months without any news. Lok became anxious and took a steamer to Shanghai to inquire everywhere. Because the address of a certain relative was unclear, he was unable to find out where they were staying. After several days, he had spent all the money he had brought. His luggage and clothes were pawned for money. With no possessions and no money to return to Hankou, he was in a desperate situation. Out of desperation, at about 11 o'clock the previous evening, he went to the Dongjiadu waterfront in Nanshi and, taking advantage of the lack of attention, jumped into the Huangpu River to seek death. A boatman nearby saw him, rushed to his rescue, and pulled him ashore, saving his life. The boatman immediately reported the incident to the sixteenth district patrol post. Officer Feng Deng'an brought him back to the responsible First Section of the First District. After a preliminary interrogation by the Section Chief, Lok explained his situation. He was ordered to prepare a written statement to be submitted to the Shanghai Municipal Police Bureau for a decision.

Robbers Armed with Weapons Seize Watermelon Boat 227

Pang A-gen, a 34-year-old from Songjiang, had been working as a boatman, recently transporting watermelons to Shanghai for sale. Yesterday afternoon, at about 2 o'clock, his boat loaded with watermelons was sailing on the Bai Miao Gang River in Longhua when he saw a boat approaching from the front at high speed. Suddenly, five men on the boat shouted loudly, forcing him to stop. Pang and the others saw that these men were fierce and armed with guns. Fearing for their safety, they immediately stopped the boat. The men jumped aboard. One of them threatened them to remain silent and watched them closely. The others began to rob dozens of watermelons and five silver dollars. They then searched the boat thoroughly but found nothing else. They then carried the stolen goods to their boat. Pang, realizing he was being robbed, tried to resist. The guard fired a shot, fortunately missing him but grazing his leg. Pang, refusing to give up, rushed forward and hugged the guard, shouting for help. At that time, officers Liu Yutian and others from the First Precinct of the Third Division of the Municipal Police Bureau's Water Patrol Team happened to be patrolling the river. Hearing the shouts, they rushed over to investigate. They arrested the gunman, seizing a rifle and three bullets. The other men took the opportunity to row away and escape. They brought the captured person, the boat owner, and the witness Sun Bao-fa back to the precinct. After a brief interrogation by the patrol officer, they were transferred to the headquarters. During a preliminary interrogation by Chief Xu, the plaintiff Pang A-gen and the witness Sun Bao-fa recounted the incident. The defendant identified himself as Wang You-heng, 22 years old, from Xiangtan, Hunan Province, and a soldier in a certain battalion. He claimed he had heard that the boat was carrying smuggled goods, so he and four colleagues brought weapons and boarded the boat in plain clothes to inspect it. The Chief questioned why, if they were on official business, they were not in uniform. He also questioned how they dared to take silver and goods from the boat and shoot at people, causing injury. He found it difficult to believe. He ordered a written statement to be prepared and submitted to the Third Section of the Shanghai Municipal Police Bureau for investigation.

P Brawl Over House Sale Results in Injuries

Dong Bu-kun, a 25-year-old factory worker from Gaoyou, residing at 878 Lime Kiln, Xiaoshadu, Shanghai West, previously built two thatched houses on a vacant lot near the residence. He moved after a short time due to insufficient space. He sold the two thatched houses to Zhou Guang-jiang from Yancheng, who paid him fifteen dollars for the building costs. However, not long after, Dong's younger brother, Bu-yun, approached Zhou demanding that the houses be returned or that Zhou pay an additional ten dollars. After repeated negotiations, Zhou refused. On the afternoon of the previous day, at 10 PM, the Dong brothers went to meet with Zhou again, urging him to move out quickly. An argument broke out, and the two sides began to fight. As a result, Bu-yun was injured in the head by Zhou and was bleeding profusely. The police were called and all were arrested and taken to the Sixth District Police Station. After an interrogation by District Chief Ren, the case, involving a dispute over the sale of a house and resulting in injuries, was documented and sent to the court for trial yesterday.

Forged Letter Used to Deceive Tobacco Shop Exposed 228

Yesterday afternoon, at about 4 o'clock, two young men, one dressed in an upper-class outfit and the other dressed like a tea server, entered the Gong He Xiang silk tobacco shop outside the Xinbei Gate. The one with the upper class outfit was wearing a long blue-grey silk gown and the other was wearing a blue striped white western cloth shirt and pants. He had a letter from the Gong Tai store in Nanhui City. The letter stated, "Please immediately pay 20 packages of Jiahe (tobacco brand) and 20 packages of Gonghe (tobacco brand) and deliver them to Mr. Yang." The shop assistant realized it was a forgery, and the seals on the letter did not match the seals on the previous letter from Gong Tai. The assistant turned the two men over to the police officer on duty, who brought them to the Second Precinct of the First District of the Municipal Police Bureau. After a brief interrogation by the station chief, they were detained pending investigation.

Illegally Moving and Selling Other People's Furniture 229

Sentenced to Imprisonment Separately

Chen Wang-shi, a woman from Ningbo residing in the Yuan Shang Li in Dongzilaihuo Street in the French Concession, reported to the French Police yesterday that Huang Chang-lin, whom she knew, colluded with Ren Yu-ting, Xue Heng-yu, and others to move all the boxes and belongings from her home and sell them while she was out. She requested an investigation. The police chief ordered a detective to arrest the three men and bring back the stolen goods to the police station. They were handed over to the French court yesterday for investigation. The plaintiff Chen Wang-shi recounted the incident. Huang Chang-lin confessed that he had been intimate with the plaintiff for many years. Recently, he went out of town for business and had no money to send back, causing the plaintiff to change her mind and work at the Ningbo prostitute house in the Asia Hotel. He learned of this upon his return to Shanghai and asked people to persuade her to live with him, but she refused. Out of anger, he moved her belongings. Ren and Xue confessed to helping with the move. Judge Zhu sentenced Huang to 14 days of imprisonment, Ren to 5 days, and Xue to a fine of 5 dollars as a warning.

Carelessness at Tianyi Film Company 230

Tea Server Burned

Yesterday morning, a fire broke out at the Tianyi Film Company, located at 53 Kunming Road. The fire started in the film processing room at 7:20 AM. The Yangshupu Fire Brigade responded immediately, but the flames were already spreading rapidly. They worked hard to extinguish the fire, and it was finally put out after about one hour and thirty minutes. Many films, materials, and equipment were burned. The buildings were also destroyed. The amount of the loss could not be immediately determined, but it was estimated to be around 5,000 silver dollars. It was reported that the films were not insured. Fortunately, some of the films were stored in a fireproof room and were not affected. During the fire, a tea server named Dai A-liang was burned on the head and face. He was rescued by firefighters and taken to the hospital for treatment.

Moving Buoys and Refurbishing Lighthouses 233

Circular from the Inspectorate of Works, Marine Department, Customs. The Inspectorate of Works has inspected the movement of the buoy in the Yao Gang Zui area of the Yangtze River, under the jurisdiction of the Jianghai Customs Tax Office. The situation is listed below. Due to the erosion of the riverbank at Yao Gang Zui, the buoy has been moved. The new location is 43 degrees east of north relative to the Langshan Pagoda, at a distance of 1.9 nautical miles, according to the compass direction. All Third Edition nautical charts published by the Marine Bureau should be corrected accordingly.

Also, circular from the Inspectorate of Works. The Inspectorate of Works has inspected the installation and refurbishment of the Qili Yue Lighthouse under the jurisdiction of the Shehai Customs Tax Office. The situation is listed below. The original light of the Qixing Island Lighthouse is scheduled to be refurbished in September. During this time, a temporary white light will be installed on the observation deck of the lighthouse, one to the north of the tower and one to the . The light is scheduled to be turned on around September 1st, at which time no further notice will be given. The temporary light is a sixth-order Asia Trade flashing light that flashes every three seconds, lasting 0.03 seconds. It can be seen from ten nautical miles in clear weather. Sometimes the conditions are similar to the original light. Details are recorded in the 19th Year of the Republic Lighthouse Buoy General Register. Once the original light has been repaired, it will be turned on. Everything will remain the same. A white light will flash rapidly twice every twenty seconds, and the light intensity will increase to 50,000 candlepower. The installed temporary light will also be removed at the same time. No further notice will be given at that time. Therefore, all ships should follow this circular and take careful note to avoid negligence. July 31, 19th Year of the Republic.

News from Various Labor Unions

Federation of Water and Electricity Workers' Unions 234

Yesterday, the preparatory committee of the Shanghai Municipal Federation of Water and Electricity Workers' Unions issued a declaration stating that the committee had been ordered to prepare for the establishment of the federation and was sworn in on July 26th. It was scheduled to begin operations and work on August 6th. However, during this preparatory period, it was feared that various sectors and labor unions in the industry were not fully aware of the true situation. Therefore, they briefly described the general outline to clarify their purpose. Since the Central Government promulgated the Labor Union Law, there is no longer a requirement for a general labor union. Therefore, they are organizing a federation of labor unions in various industries to test the results. If the results are excellent, then they will consider federations of labor unions in other industries. The federation was established at a time when the country is facing many difficulties and the front is working hard to kill the enemy. The rear should be tightly organized to prevent villains from jumping out and disrupting the revolutionary front. Therefore, the federation will do its best to prepare for the establishment of the municipal federation of water and electricity workers' unions in three months, in accordance with the organizational rules, in order to achieve a complete preparation. All organizations in the industry should regard the federation as a real need and the only group, and should work together in harmony to achieve success, so that the industry can be united and the unity can be expanded to prepare for common interests and seek the development of the future. The future of the party and the country and the future of the labor movement all depend on it. This declaration is made.

Local News 2

Zhang Wenqing Not Sentenced to Death 241

Sentence Changed to Life Imprisonment

Chen Hengcai Sentenced to Death

Zhang Fusheng, the former magistrate of the Qing Dynasty, died many years ago. His eldest daughter, Wenqing, is now 24 years old and has not yet married. On January 25 of this year, Zhang's concubine, Ms. Su, was killed in her residence on Biande Road. After the incident, the police investigation showed that Wenqing had instigated Chen Hengcai to conspire with Gao Jintang and Yao Yonggui to commit the crime. They were taken to court and sentenced to death. Zhang and the others refused to accept the verdict and hired lawyers Wang Yintai and Wang Chuanbi to appeal to the Second Branch of the Jiangsu Higher Court. The appeal brief was several thousand words long, elaborating on the facts and the law. The most important points are as follows: (1) A comparison of the probative value of the police statements, the first trial testimony, and the testimony of the Second Branch. (2) The three essential elements of constituting an instigation offense. (3) Whether Zhang Wenqing had a motive to instigate the murder of her stepmother. (4) Why Chen Hengcai wanted to kill Zhang Su-shi. Yesterday morning was the date for the second trial of the case. The police brought the defendants to the First Tribunal of the Higher Court. The lawyers for all parties, Wang Yintai, Wang Chuanbi, Wang Yaotang, Jiang Rongfan, Gang Wu Zhiping, and others, were present in court. At nine o'clock, Presiding Judge Song Yuan, Judge Du Fuyue, and Chief Prosecutor Wang Zhennan arrived in succession. Judge Song read the judgment, stating that the original judgment was reversed. Chen Hengcai was sentenced to death for the crime of jointly premeditating murder. Zhang Wenqing, Yao Yonggui, and Gao Jintang were sentenced to life imprisonment for the crime of joint murder, and all were deprived of their civil rights for life. After the judgment was read, the police took the defendants out of the courtroom. At this time, Chen Hengcai not only showed no signs of sorrow, but also sang loudly. The song he sang was neither Peking opera nor Kunqu opera, but a folk song from northern Jiangsu. Those who heard it were amused. The police were satisfied with the verdict and will not appeal further. It is not yet known whether the defendants will all plead guilty or appeal to the third trial.

Unwrapping the Diaper Reveals a Boy Instead of a Girl

The Girl's Testimony: "Don't Say"

Conflicting Accounts of Origin from the Couple

Ten Men, Women, and Children Apprehended

The Taikoo Company's Taiyuan steamer, docked at the Taikoo Wharf in the French Concession, was about to set sail at 6:00 AM yesterday morning when Chen Shaoting and Lin Yongfang, investigators from the Women and Children Relief Association, together with Hua Detective Jiang Changsheng and Cheng Yongnian from the Water Police, boarded the ship for inspection. Whispering Quietly 243

accompanied by a young girl and three boys. Each of the two women was holding a baby. Finding their behavior suspicious, they were immediately interrogated. Another man, claiming to be Hu Kewang, 34 years old, a stone mason from Changxing, said that his brother had opened a stone shop in Xiamen and had written to him asking him to go there to work. Therefore, he was traveling to Xiamen with his sister-in-law (referring to the two women) and children, and there was nothing else. One of the women, claiming to be Ms. Hu Zhang, 29 years old, from Changxing, said that she was Hu Kewang's wife. Seeing that she was

Holding a Baby 247

the police chief, in order to investigate the case, asked her quickly whether the child was a boy or a girl. Upon hearing this, the woman tried to open the diaper (i.e. the cloth diaper bag), but was stopped by the police chief. Seeing that her plan had failed, the woman hastily replied that it was a girl. revealing that it was indeed a male child. The woman's face turned red and she lowered her head without a word. she was hiding that she was unwilling to say. If she was suffering, they could find a way to help her. However, the girl still said "Don't Say". Suspicious Points 250

(1) Chen Jianwu first claimed that his wife (i.e., Ms. Zheng) was from the same village (i.e., Changxing), but Ms. Zheng claimed to be from Wenzhou. The First Time Destroyed the House and Injured People

This Time Only a Near Miss

On June 14, the Shanghai Arsenal test-fired a shell at the Wusong Fortress on the northeast coast of Taiwan. A shell landed on the home of villager Chen Fenglai, destroying the house and killing Chen's mother, Ms. Ying.
