Chen Fenglai happened to be holding a memorial service for his mother on that day, and relatives and friends were gathered. Unexpectedly, a shell fell from the sky, landing in Chen Fenglai's home for the second time, piercing the wall. Fortunately, the shell did not explode, so no one was injured. However, Chen's relatives and others rushed out of the house in a panic.

Empress of Japan Changes Anchorage to Wusong 252

The Changxing Company's newly built largest new Pacific liner, the Empress of Japan, with a displacement of 33,000 tons and a speed of 23 nautical miles per hour, was originally scheduled to arrive in Shanghai from London on the ninth of this month and berth at the Yongdong Blue Funnel Wharf. An invitation was extended to all sectors to visit the ship from 3:00 PM. This matter has been noted in this newspaper. It is now known that the ship's draft is too deep and the ship's hull is too large. The company has changed its plan. After arriving in Shanghai on the ninth, it will not berth at the Blue Funnel Wharf for the time being, but will anchor at the Wusong Estuary. The company will provide three small boats to pick up guests at the New Customs Wharf at 2:00 PM on the same afternoon and transport them to Wusong to board the large plate. The Shanghai class owner will visit them and serve tea and refreshments.

Yu Qingyu Appeals Against Wu Jianguang and Others 255

Yu Qingyu previously sued the famous astrologer Wu Jianguang and others for fraud in the Shanghai Special District Court. The presiding judge Feng Shide declared the defendants not guilty in court. This has been repeatedly noted in this newspaper. It is now known that the plaintiff Yu Qingyu has hired lawyer Zhang Chongding to prepare an appeal, as the appeal period is about to expire. This shows that the rumor that the plaintiff and defendant have reached a settlement is not true. The appeal prepared by lawyer Zhang is extracted below.

Criminal Appeal 256

Appellant: Yu Qingyu

Appellees: Wu Jianguang, Wang Yonghai, Chai Caifa, Chai Caigao, Wang Zhenhai, et al. (ages, native places, and addresses omitted)

Regarding the matter of disagreeing with the first instance acquittal of the defendants and therefore legally filing an appeal: The appellant, in the first instance, brought a private prosecution against the defendants for fraud. On July 28th of this year, the appellant received the esteemed court's judgment, the main text of which reads: Wu Jianguang, Wang Yonghai, Chai Caifa, Chai Caigao, and Wang Zhenhai are all not guilty. After receiving the judgment, the appellant found it truly difficult to accept and is therefore filing an appeal within the statutory period. The reasons for disagreement are respectfully presented below:

(1) The greatest error in the original judgment lies in its determination that, although astrology involves superstition, there is no specific article in criminal law to punish it. However, Article 363 of the criminal law clearly stipulates that if one intends to illegally possess something and uses fraudulent means to induce another person to hand over their property, it constitutes the crime of fraud. In this case, the appellees make a living from astrology, and Wu Jianguang and others openly admit this. The stars are a phenomenon of the natural world, and the Earth is also a planet. What connection can the movements of the stars possibly have with the fate of humans on Earth? Furthermore, a person's birth year, month, day, and hour have no mathematical formula that can determine their destiny. The appellees use this baseless deception as a means of making a living. If this is not a fraudulent trick, what is it? Moreover, they use dangerous language, trying to quickly fool ignorant women into believing them. If this is not inducing people to hand over their property, what is it? Yet the judgment says that criminal law has no specific article to punish it. This is truly like what Master Zi said: "Clearly observing the tip of an autumn hair but not seeing a cartload of firewood." This is the first reason for disagreement.

(2) The appellee Wu Jianguang in this case engages in supernatural trickery opposite the Hongmiao Temple in Nanjing, making a din of drums every day. Passersby all know this. The appellant's lawyer, upon briefly glancing at the account books he presented, immediately discovered entries for 21 yuan, 36 yuan, 56 yuan, and 36 yuan from August 11th to 13th. It can be imagined that he habitually engages in fraud. Yet the original judgment determined that the testimony of the appellant's wife was not credible because there was no Chen Xing real person. However, it is not known how many account books Wu Jianguang, whose business is booming, may have at the same time. Criminal proceedings prioritize discovering the truth. The truth of this case has already been discovered, yet the original judgment picked up on minor details in the testimony to declare the defendant not guilty. How can this possibly be convincing? Chai Shaofa and Chai Caigao hired the blind Wang Yonghai, using the name of his deceased father, Chai Wenzhong, to open a divination hall and share the profits. A receipt written by Chai Caifa is evidence. Yet the original judgment, based on the defendants only admitting to receiving six jiao of foreign currency, declared them not guilty. However, in law, the only question is whether a crime was committed. Even if it is only a small silver coin, if the elements of the crime are present, it should be punished accordingly. Although Wang Zhenhai did not admit to knowing the scriptures and incantations, this is also just empty words of denial. The appellant has already presented evidence, but the original trial summarily dismissed it, making it difficult for the appellant to accept. This is another reason for disagreement.

Based on the above reasons, the appellant respectfully requests that the esteemed court overturn the original judgment and punish each appellee according to the provisions of Article 363 of the Criminal Law, as well as Article 364 of the same law, to demonstrate party governance and follow the trend of the times, for the sake of public convenience.

Respectfully submitted to the Shanghai Special District Local Court of Jiangsu Province.

Submitted by: Yu Qingyu

Drawn up by: Lawyer Zhang Chongding

Yesterday morning at about 10:00 AM, the Shanghai-Hangzhou Railway's New Longhua Station dispatched laborers to repair and deepen a ditch because it was clogged. Jin Yousun Cannot Find His Wife

Has Another Argument with His Mother-in-Law

Jin Yousun, who works in a grain shop on Wangjia Wharf in the South Market, married into the Jin family of Nanhui as a live-in son-in-law to Jin Zhou's daughter, Jin Jin. Because he often works in Shanghai, his wife was left alone, leading to an affair with Zhang Yongmei, an assistant clerk who is a civil servant. When the affair was discovered, the Nanhui County sentenced each of the adulterous couple to three months of imprisonment. Zhang and Jin Jin did not accept the sentence and appealed to the local court, which upheld the original judgment. They were imprisoned in the Caohejing Third Prison. Yesterday, Jin arrived at the prison gate at 8:00 AM to wait for his wife to be released and take her home. Unexpectedly, two cars were already waiting in front of the prison gate. Soon after, Zhang Yongmei and Jin Jin were released together and left in the cars. At that time, Jin Zhou was also in front of the prison gate. Jin Yousun immediately stepped forward to stop them but was beaten. Helpless, he took Jin Zhou to the Third Branch of the Sixth District police station. Yesterday, she was transferred to the local court. According to Jin Zhou, "My daughter was originally a live-in bride, so of course she should return home with me. She is indeed at my home now. Jin Yousun can come to my home, but my daughter cannot go to his home. Zhang Yongmei did not go with her." Fire on Yuanfang Road 259

Another Woman Dies from Severe Injuries

At about 1:00 AM the day before yesterday, a fire broke out at 133 Donggui Lane, Yuanfang Road, Hongkou, when a resident named Li Tianmin, a Cantonese man, was carelessly preparing opium. The fire quickly spread to the neighboring 132 and burned to death four men and women on the spot, and injured six men and women. The injured were sent to Tongren Hospital. Afterwards, firefighters found the bodies in the fire and carried them to the Forensic Examination Office on Feilun Road, but their faces were burned beyond recognition and it was impossible to determine their identities or genders. The day before yesterday, the Special District Court dispatched Prosecutor Xu Mu to the Forensic Examination Office to confirm that the two corpses were burned to death and that no relatives had claimed the bodies. Therefore, he ordered that they be temporarily placed in the Pushan Cemetery, marked with the date of death, pending identification by relatives. That afternoon, detectives from the Hongkou Police Station found another body in Dachang and learned his name was Wang Gendi. At the same time, Tongren Hospital called the police to report that one of the injured women, Wang Wu, had succumbed to the fire's toxins and died. The police then sent her body to the Forensic Examination Office as well. Yesterday morning, the Special Court again dispatched Prosecutor Guo Huaipu to the Forensic Examination Office. Ye Kunrong arrived and claimed that Wang Wu was his maternal aunt and Wang Gendi was his cousin, and that he would claim their bodies. Mr. Guo approved this and ordered that the two bodies be handed over to Ye Kunrong for burial. The arsonist has now been prosecuted by the police.

Woman Requests Divorce Due to Intolerable Abuse 260

Reconciliation Achieved in Court, Divorce Granted

He Qian, a woman from Nanjing, is 29 years old. She married He Yushan, a man from Shaoxing, in 1921. After she married into the family, her husband despised her because of her appearance. As a result, their feelings for each other faded. More recently, He had an affair and treated her like a thorn in his side. Friends and relatives had previously stepped in to mediate, providing her with living expenses of 10 yuan per month. However, this was only empty talk. Unable to endure the suffering, she hired Lawyer Jin to file a lawsuit for divorce in the local court. The lawsuit stated that she had been abused and abandoned by the defendant, He Yushan, and that he had failed to provide for her. She requested the court to grant a divorce. As the plaintiff is a weak woman, how can she live independently? Even if the defendant agreed to pay the promised amount monthly, it would be difficult to survive. Furthermore, he cut off all support, leaving her starving and freezing. In July, she argued with him about this, and the defendant, being violent, became furious and beat her, causing her to be injured and nearly die. Neighbors rescued her and she fled back to her mother's home. The next day, she reported the injuries to the prosecutor's office of the court. As the defendant avoided appearing in court, it was ordered that if the plaintiff saw the defendant, she should immediately arrest him and bring him to trial. The plaintiff was unlucky in marriage and had no choice but to divorce in order to save her life. Yesterday morning, Presiding Judge Zhao Zhenhai specially opened the Second Court to hear the case. The plaintiff, He Qian, testified, "I married the defendant at the age of 20. We did not have any children." (Question) "Have you always been on good terms?" (Answer) "He dislikes my appearance, so we are not on good terms." (Question) "How much can you earn doing work each month?" (Answer) "More than ten yuan." (Question) "Why do you want a divorce?" (Answer) "He doesn't support me." (Question) "Do you live together now?" (Answer) "We separated on March 28th last year. He took my belongings away, leaving me with no place to live. I found him this April, but he and his mistress beat me." (Question) "What is his mistress's name?" (Answer) "Her name is Shun Di. They injured my right eye, left arm, and lower abdomen. The prosecutor's office examined the injuries and issued a government order." The defendant, He Yushan, testified that he was 33 years old and did not want a divorce. (Question) "Do you have a mistress?" (Answer) "She is not a mistress, she is a neighbor." (Question) "What is Shun Di's last name?" (Answer) "I don't know. She has a man who works in the electrical certificate business." (Question) "Did you beat the plaintiff?" (Answer) "No, I did not." (Question) "If you didn't beat her, how did she get injured?" The defendant was speechless. Judge Zhao first attempted to reconcile the two parties. As a result, divorce was granted. Judge Zhao drafted a reconciliation record. Afterwards, the man and woman were free to marry as they pleased. Both parties signed the agreement and left the court.

Original Sentence Upheld for Two Women

Chen Zhang, a woman from Suqian, killed her son Mingjian (30 years old) because he did not work and only loved smoking and gambling. Father-in-Law Regrets Marriage Because Son-in-Law is Poor 263

Yu Yanyu, 49 years old from Hubei, rents a house at 124 Lujiazhai, Pudong and runs a noodle shop. He has a daughter who is of age and was betrothed to Li Shengdi, a fellow villager, since she was young. They have not yet married. Li, now 23, works as an employee in a noodle shop at 7 Luban Road, Lujiawan Road in the French Concession. His wages are barely enough to make ends meet, and he is too poor to marry and start a family. Recently, he was suspended from his job by the shop owner for something and had nowhere to go. He had no choice but to cross the river to his father-in-law's place the day before yesterday afternoon and ask him to take him in. He was willing to temporarily work as a shop assistant to find a place to stay. Unexpectedly, as soon as Yu heard Li's words, his face turned cold and he firmly refused to acknowledge him as his son-in-law. The two sides then clashed, and Li destroyed some of Yu's shop's items. The police from the Fourth Squad of the Police Department arrived and took Yu and Li to the Third District Police Station. Yu stated that although his daughter was promised to Li as a wife when she was young, they had not gone through the engagement ceremony. He now saw that Li could barely support himself, let alone support a wife, so he denied that Li was his son-in-law. Li stated that there was indeed a matchmaker proving that Yu had betrothed his daughter to him as his wife. He now sees that I am poor and intends to break the engagement and asked for help. The district chief verified the statements and, as the case involved a marriage dispute, he was unable to handle it and ordered both parties to file a lawsuit in court.

Is There a Suspicion of False Accusation in the Case of Accusing People of Enticing and Killing a Woman? 264

Plaintiff Detained in Police Station for Investigation

Zhang Jinfa, from Jiangbei, reported to the Fourth Branch of the Fifth District police station the day before yesterday that Zhang Wanchang and his mother, Zhang Gu, who live at 303 Huade Road in the concession, enticed his sister, Zhao Zhang, to a deserted area near Gaolang Bridge in the Chinese area in June 1925 and killed her. The district sent detectives to Gengshu Pu Police Station to assist in detaining Zhang Wanchang and Zhang Gu. Yesterday morning, they were sent to the Third Criminal Court of the Special District Court. The police lawyer, Zhang Tianyin, stated that the allegations reported by Zhang Jinfa were unfounded. The police found that the two defendants have always been law-abiding. Later, Shi Lantian, a detective from the Public Security Bureau, complained that a murder did occur at the end of June of that year. The body was examined by the local court, and no relatives came to claim it. Therefore, an official letter was submitted for inspection. Furthermore, the plaintiff, Zhang Jinfa, complained that the deceased, Zhao Zhang, was my sister. She married a man named Cao from Zhenjiang. Her brother-in-law died in September 1924. The defendant, Zhang Gu, came to Shanghai with her from Zhenjiang. Afterwards, there was no news of her. Therefore, when she was killed, I did not know about it. It was not until recently that a certain person living with the defendant told me about it that I knew about it. Therefore, I reported it to the bureau. When questioned, the defendant Zhang Wanchang stated that he was a painter in Hong Kong at the time and knew nothing about the accusations. Zhang Gu also denied the allegations and claimed that she was being falsely accused. Furthermore, the police lawyer claimed that many of the things reported by the plaintiff at the police station were inaccurate and requested the court to order the plaintiff to be temporarily detained at the police station for a detailed investigation. If it is a false accusation, the police will file a public prosecution. It was also heard that the plaintiff had made similar false reports to the Public Security Bureau. After Judge Feng Shide verified the statements, he ordered that the two reports be returned separately for investigation by the local court and the case file of Zhang Gu's suspected murder. Zhang Jinfa was temporarily detained in the police station pending investigation.

Opening of Guo Ju'an's Appeal Case 265

A Major Debate on the Issue of Legal Persons Arises

The American-owned Chase Bank previously sued Guo Ju'an in the former Provisional Court for failing to perform his guarantee debt of over 64,000 taels. The court ruled against the defendant. Guo, dissatisfied, filed an appeal with the Sino-Foreign Civil Appeal Office attached to the Ministry of Foreign Affairs. Until the end of last year, the Ministry ordered the abolition of the Appeal Office, and the Appeal Office was eliminated along with it. However, the case had not yet been tried. The case files of this appeal were initially preserved by the Shanghai Office of the Ministry of Foreign Affairs. Recently, the judicial authorities decided that all unresolved appeal cases would be handled by the Second Branch of the Jiangsu High Court. Guo's appeal case was heard yesterday by Presiding Judge Hu and Judges Li and Ye. The appellant's lawyer first raised the issue of legal persons and requested that it be resolved first. The reason was roughly that Chase Bank had not registered with the Chinese government and had not obtained legal person status, so it should not have the capacity to litigate. This argument was similar to the one made by lawyer Zhang Rongxi in the case of Mitsui & Co. suing He Gengxing and others. However, the lawyer for the appellee, Chase Bank, seemed to have anticipated this issue and used the name of Chase's manager in the response. However, the appellant's lawyer then stated that its main body was incorrect. The first instance was signed by Chase, and the second instance cannot be changed at will. Therefore, the two lawyers debated each other from morning to noon without addressing the merits of the case. The court stated that the point of contention regarding legal persons raised by the appellant did not require much debate because the appellee had already changed to using a natural person's name. However, as it was time to adjourn, it was ordered that the case be rescheduled for another hearing.

Letter 274

To the Editor,

In the suicide news of Hao Futian in your newspaper yesterday, there was a statement that "the general manager of the [Blank] Raisin Company published an advertisement to recruit managers. Mr. [Blank] Ti Fang collected 1,000 yuan to apply for the job. Unexpectedly, a few days later, [Blank] absconded with the money due to debt." After investigation, our company's general manager has never absconded. No other employee has absconded due to debt. Furthermore, we have never heard of a [Blank] Ti Fang. He must not be an employee of our company. Therefore, we are writing to request a correction to be published in a prominent position in your newspaper.

Sincerely,

Ministry of Education Revises 275

Regulations on the Organization of Primary and Secondary Schools and County Education Bureaus in Jiangsu Province

Primary School Principals Manage School Administration Under the Direction of the Department Head and Middle School Principals

Students Expelled from Middle School May Be Given Certificates Permitting Transfer to Another School

The Words "Provisional" Should Be Added to the Regulations on the Organization of Education Bureaus in Each County

The Jiangsu Provincial Department of Education recently promulgated the regulations on the appointment, dismissal, and treatment of principals of provincial primary and secondary schools, the provisional regulations on the organization of primary and secondary schools, and the regulations on the organization of education bureaus in each county. The Jiangsu Provincial Government sent a request to the Ministry of Education to review and register the regulations. Yesterday, the Ministry of Education replied to the Provincial Government with three points of revision to the original regulations. The three points of revision are excerpted below:

After reviewing the "Regulations on the Appointment, Dismissal, and Treatment of Principals of Provincial Secondary Schools in Jiangsu Province" and the "Provisional Regulations on the Appointment, Dismissal, and Treatment of Principals of County Primary Schools in Jiangsu Province," there are no discrepancies and they may be registered. The remaining regulations should be revised in accordance with the following points: (1) The "Provisional Regulations on the Appointment, Dismissal, and Treatment of Principals of Provincial Secondary School Experimental Primary Schools in Jiangsu Province" and the "Provisional Regulations on the Organization of Provincial Secondary School Experimental Primary Schools in Jiangsu Province" are both prefixed with the words "Provincial Secondary School." Furthermore, Article 13 of the "Provisional Regulations on the Organization of Provincial Secondary Schools in Jiangsu Province" stipulates the establishment of experimental primary schools, indicating that experimental primary schools are part of the organization of provincial secondary schools. However, Article 13 of the "Provisional Regulations on the Organization of Provincial Secondary Schools in Jiangsu Province" stipulates that the principal of the experimental primary school reports to the principal of the secondary school, while Article 2 of the "Provisional Regulations on the Organization of Provincial Secondary School Experimental Primary Schools in Jiangsu Province" stipulates that "the principal of the experimental primary school reports to the head of the Department of Education." The provisions seem to be inconsistent, and the regulations on the relationship between the experimental primary school and the provincial secondary school also seem to be slightly unclear. The Ministry proposes the following revisions: In the "Provisional Regulations on the Appointment, Dismissal, and Treatment of Principals of Provincial Secondary School Experimental Primary Schools in Jiangsu Province," delete Articles 1 and 2. Article 1 pertains to organization and can be included in the "Provisional Regulations on the Organization of Principals of Provincial Secondary School Experimental Primary Schools in Jiangsu Province." Article 2 pertains to the duties of the principal and can be stipulated in the "Detailed Rules for the Service of Principals of Experimental Primary Schools." Both are unrelated to appointment, dismissal, and treatment. (2) Add an item to Article 3 of the "Provisional Regulations on the Organization of Provincial Secondary Schools in Jiangsu Province": "Each middle school teacher training department shall establish an experimental primary school to provide students with practical training and experimental primary school education. Its organizational regulations will be formulated separately." In Article 13, do not add the five words "Head of the Department of Education and" to "reports to." (3) Change the "Provisional Regulations on the Organization of Provincial Secondary School Experimental Primary Schools in Jiangsu Province" to the first article of the "Provisional Regulations on the Appointment, Dismissal, and Treatment of Principals of Provincial Secondary School Experimental Primary Schools in Jiangsu Province" as Article 1 of these regulations. Sequentially change the numbers of the articles after the original Article 1. Change the original Article 3 to "Article 4: The experimental primary school shall have one principal who manages school administration under the direction of the Head of the Department of Education and the principal of this middle school." (2) Students who are expelled from school are generally deficient in conduct, academic performance, or physical education. If they are all prohibited from applying to transfer to another school, then these students will never have the opportunity to enroll and further their studies, which seems unsatisfactory. In Article 17 of the "Provisional Regulations on Admission, Transfer, Withdrawal, Suspension, and Continuation of Studies in County Secondary Schools in Jiangsu Province," delete the original Article 18 and renumber Articles 18 to 23 as Articles 17 to 22. The first item of Article 22 (i.e., the original Article 23) must be changed to the fifth item. The original items 2, 3, 4, and 5 are changed to items 1, 2, 3, and 4. After Article 22 (i.e., the original Article 23), add an article as Article 23, which reads: "Students who are expelled due to the circumstances of the preceding articles may be given a transcript and certificate of completion by the original school, except for those whose circumstances are serious due to the circumstances of the first item (i.e., the original second item)." Also, in Article 24, change the words "Article 21" and "Article 23" to "Article 20" and "Article 22." (3) In the "Regulations on the Organization of Education Bureaus in Each County of Jiangsu Province," add the words "Provisional" under the words "Regulations." The above is approved for reference. It is requested that these review opinions be examined and that a response be provided. This is sent to the Jiangsu Provincial Government.

Shanghai Private School Screening Test Subjects Announced 276

The Ministry of Education recently announced the subjects for the screening tests for graduates and former students of private vocational schools and above within Shanghai that are unregistered or have been closed. Although the breakdown by school level and college is very detailed, the test subjects and questions are quite easy. The subjects are as follows:

(A) Basic Subjects 277

Five subjects will be tested: (1) Party Principles (2) Chinese Language (3) Foreign Language (choose one from English, French, or Japanese) (4) Social Sciences (choose one from five subjects: Chinese and foreign history, Chinese and foreign geography, outlines of political science, outlines of economics, outlines of sociology) (5) Natural Sciences (choose one from four subjects: mathematics, physics, chemistry, biology)

(D) University Specialized Subjects 278

Majors and vocational schools will test three subjects for those who have completed one or two academic years, four subjects for those who have completed three academic years, and five subjects for those who have completed four academic years (i.e., graduates). 1. College of Arts (1) Chinese Literature Department (referred to as "one year" for those who have completed one academic year or less): Introduction to Literature, Philology, Chinese Grammar. (Referred to as "two years" for those who have completed two academic years or less): Same as one year. (Referred to as "three years" for those who have completed three academic years or less): In addition to two years, add Rhetoric. (Referred to as "four years" for those who have completed four academic years or less): In addition to three years, add History of Chinese Literature. (2) English Department (One Year): English Composition, Translation, Anthology of Famous English and American Writers. (Two Years): English Composition, Translation, History of English Literature or English Minor Language. (Three Years): Choose four out of five subjects: English Composition, English Novel, History of English Literature, English Drama, Second Foreign Language at the one-year level. (Four Years): Choose five out of six subjects: English Novel, History of English Literature, English Drama, History of Western Literature, English Poetry, Second Foreign Language at the two-year level. (3) Philosophy Department (One Year and Two Years): Introduction to Philosophy, History of Western Philosophy, Logic. (Three Years): In addition to the above two years, add Epistemology. (Four Years): In addition to the above three years, add Modern Western Philosophy. (4) History Department (One Year and Two Years): General History of China, General History of the West, General History of the East. (Three Years): General History of China, General History of the West, History of Chinese Culture, History of Western Culture. (Four Years): Modern History of China, Modern History of the West, History of Chinese Culture, History of Western Culture, General Theory of Historiography. (5) Sociology Department (One Year and Two Years): Introduction to Sociology, Social Psychology, Family Problems or Population Problems. (Three Years): In addition to the above two years, add History of Social Thought. (Four Years): Introduction to Sociology, History of Social Thought, History of Sociology, Social Investigation, Rural Sociology or Urban Sociology. 2. College of Science (1) Mathematics Department (One Year): Elementary Analytical Geometry, Advanced Algebra, Elementary Calculus. (Two Years): Advanced Analytical Geometry, Advanced Algebra, Elementary Equations, Higher Algebra. (Three Years): Advanced Calculus, Advanced Analytical Geometry (Solid Geometry), Differential Equations, Higher Algebra. (Four Years): Real Variable Function Theory, Complex Variable Function Theory, Partial Differential Equations, Differential Geometry, Analytical Mechanics. (2) Physics Department (One Year): Analytical Geometry, Advanced Algebra, General Physics. (Two Years): Calculus, General Physics, Inorganic Chemistry. (Three Years): Differential Equations, Qualitative Analysis, and choose one from Mechanics, Optics, Electricity, Thermodynamics. (Four Years): Theoretical Mechanics, Thermodynamics, Optics, Advanced Electricity, Modern Physics. (Experimental reports must be submitted for all physics courses in each year.) (3) Chemistry Department (One Year): Analytical Geometry, Advanced Algebra, Inorganic Chemistry. (Two Years): Differential Calculus, General Physics, Inorganic Chemistry. (Three Years): Calculus, University General Physics, Quantitative Analysis, Organic Chemistry. (Four Years): Calculus, University General Physics, Quantitative Analysis, Organic Chemistry, Theoretical Chemistry. (Experimental reports must be submitted for all chemistry courses in each year.) (4) Biology Department (One Year): General Zoology, General Botany, General Chemistry. (Two Years, Zoology Group): General Botany, Comparative Anatomy, Animal Taxonomy. (Two Years, Botany Group): General Zoology, Plant Anatomy, Plant Taxonomy. (Three Years, Zoology Group): In addition to the above two years, add Animal Physiology. (Three Years, Botany Group): In addition to the above two years, add Plant Physiology. (Four Years, Zoology Group): In addition to the above three years, add Histology and Embryology. (Four Years, Botany Group): In addition to the above three years, add Plant Morphology. (Choose one group from the second year onwards.) (5) Psychology Department (One Year and Two Years): General Psychology, Experimental Psychology, Comparative Psychology, Physiological Basis of Psychology. (Three Years): General Psychology (including Advanced General Psychology), Experimental Psychology (including Advanced Experimental Psychology), Comparative Psychology or Physiological Basis of Psychology, Applied Psychology (including Educational Psychology, etc.) or Abnormal Psychology. (Four Years): Advanced General Psychology (including General Psychology), Advanced Experimental Psychology (including Experimental Psychology, with experimental work or description of one or two experiments), Comparative Psychology or Physiological Basis of Psychology, Applied Psychology, Abnormal Psychology. (3) Law School (1) Economics Department (One Year): Economics (required), Political Science, Introduction to Law, Monetary Science, Public Finance (choose two from the above four subjects). (Two Years): Economics, Economic Geography, Economic History, Public Finance, Money and Banking, History of Economic Thought (choose three from the above six subjects). (Three Years): Advanced Economics, History of Economic Thought, Public Finance, Money and Banking, Cooperatives, Socialism and Social Movements, Economic History (choose four from the above seven subjects). (Four Years): Same as three years, choose five subjects from the seven subjects. (2) Political Science Department (One Year): Political Science, World Political History, Economics. (Two Years): Constitution, Political Systems of Europe and America, Sociology. (Three Years): Administrative Law, History of Political Thought in Europe and America, International Public Law, Public Finance. (Four Years): International Politics, Political Parties of Various Countries, Diplomatic History of China, Local Autonomy, Modern Social Problems and Social Policy. (3) Law Department (One Year and Two Years): General Principles of Civil Law, General Principles of Criminal Law, Roman Law or Civil Law - Obligations. (Three Years): General Principles of Civil Law, General Principles of Criminal Law, Civil Law - General Principles, Criminal Law - Specific Offenses. (Four Years): Civil Law - Obligations, Civil Law - Real Rights, Criminal Law - General Principles, Criminal Law - Specific Offenses, Civil or Criminal Procedure Law. 4. College of Education (1) Education Department (One Year and Two Years): Introduction to Education or Principles of Education, Psychology or Outline of Educational Psychology, History of Education or Teaching Methods. (Three Years): Choose one subject from each of the following four categories: 1. Philosophy of Education, Sociology of Education. 2. Educational Psychology, Child Psychology. 3. Elementary School Teaching Methods, Secondary School Teaching Methods, Modern Educational Trends. 4. Educational Administration, Comparative Education, etc. Elementary Education, Secondary Education, Normal Education, Vocational Education, Adult Education. (Four Years): In addition to the above three years, choose one subject from the following three subjects: Intelligence Testing, Educational Testing, Educational Statistics. (2) Educational Psychology Department (One Year and Two Years): General Psychology, Educational Psychology, Principles of Education or Outline. (Three Years): In addition to the above two years, add Experimental Educational Psychology (including Learning Psychology, Intelligence Testing) or one subject from Child Psychology or Adolescent Psychology. (Four Years): In addition to the above two years, add one Experimental Educational Psychology (including Learning Psychology, Intelligence Testing with practical work or description of one or two experiments), 2. Child Psychology or Adolescent Psychology. 5. College of Engineering (1) Civil Engineering Department (One Year): Analytical Geometry, Calculus, General Physics (Mechanics), and submit Machine Drawing or Descriptive Geometry and Surveying Notebook. (Two Years): Calculus, General Physics (Optics, Electricity, Thermodynamics), Statics, and submit Machine Drawing or Descriptive Geometry and Surveying Notebook. (Three Years): Soil Mechanics, Hydraulics, Strength of Materials, General Electrical Engineering or Steam Engine, and submit Advanced Surveying Notebook. (Four Years): Reinforced Concrete, Railway Surveying (required), Urban Water Supply, Hydrometry, Railway Engineering, Road Engineering, River Engineering, Canal Engineering, Irrigation Engineering, Harbor Engineering, Sewage Engineering (choose two from the above nine subjects), and submit General Bridge Design and one selected subject project report. (2) Mechanical Engineering Department (One Year): Analytical Geometry, Calculus, General Physics (Mechanics), and submit Descriptive Geometry. (Two Years): Calculus, General Physics (Optics, Electricity, Thermodynamics), Statics, and submit Machine Drawing. (Three Years): Principles of Machinery, Steam Engine, Thermodynamics, Strength of Materials, and submit Experimental Report and Mechanical Project. (Four Years): Hydraulics, Electrical Engineering, Power Plant (required), Advanced Steam Engineering, Internal Combustion Engine, Railway Mechanical Engineering (choose one from the above three subjects), and submit one selected subject project and experimental report. (6) College of Commerce The test subjects for all departments in the first and second years are the same. (One Year): Bookkeeping and Accounting, Principles of Economics, General Commercial Theory or Money and Banking. (Two Years): Bookkeeping and Accounting, Principles of Economics, Money and Banking. The subjects for the third and fourth years are specified by department: (1) Banking Department (Three Years): Statistics, Commercial Law, Commercial Banking, Bank Accounting. (Four Years): Commercial Credit, Foreign Exchange, Investment Science, Banking System, Chinese Financial Problems. (2) Accounting Department (Three Years): Statistics, Commercial Law, Commercial Mathematics, Advanced Accounting. (Four Years): Cost Accounting, Auditing, Government Accounting, Accounting System, Railway Accounting. (3) International Trade Department (Three Years): Statistics, Commercial Law, Transportation Science, Principles of Foreign Trade. (Four Years): Market Science, Sales Science, Advertising Science, Foreign Exchange, International Commercial Policy. (Four Years): Labor Problems, Industrial Management, Employee Management, Office Management, Railway Management. (Four Years): Choose five subjects from the departments in the same year. (7) Medical School (One Year and Two Years): Anatomy (including Histology, etc.), Physiology (including Biochemistry), Pathology (including Bacteriology). (Three Years): Internal Medicine (including Diagnostics, etc.), Surgery (including Dermatology and Venereology, etc.), Obstetrics and Gynecology, Hygiene. Zhang Zhongdao Appointed Acting Director of the Beijing Municipal Education Bureau 280

Liu Pingjiang, Director of the Nanjing Municipal Education Bureau, requested to resign after his term as acting director expired, which was approved by Mayor Wei. Zhang Zhongdao, Director of the Social Affairs Bureau, was appointed as acting director. It is understood that Mr. Zhang will take office on the 8th. It is also said that the new acting director of the Social Affairs Bureau, Huang Zengyue, will also take office on the same day.

Local News

Municipal Education Bureau Organizes High School Graduation Retake Examination Committee 281

The Shanghai Municipal Education Bureau, after conducting the junior high school entrance examination and high school proctored examination, has stipulated retake examination measures for some students who did not participate in the examination due to illness or failed the examination, and has informed the schools. As the retake examination is approaching, the Education Bureau has actively prepared and invited Ni Wenya, Tang Shouqian, Chuan Jitien, Zhou Junshang, Zhang Huibao, Peng Yanyan, Dai Ying, Yao Zhibi, Zhang Yanggao, Shen Yuguang, and Zhang Duanzhen to serve as members of the high school graduation retake examination committee. The first municipal meeting was held a few days ago and decided: (A) Candidates should take care of their own lunch. (B) The examination venue will be at Wuben Girls' High School, with the high school in the auditorium of the middle school department, and the junior high school in the auditorium of the elementary school department and the teachers' classroom. (C) Candidates' names and schools should be written on the examination papers, without using numbers. (D) Candidates should submit photos at the time of the examination. The name of the school and the name of the candidate should be written on the back, as well as the subjects for which the retake examination is being taken. Before each examination, the proctor will leave a name to match the photo and then issue the examination paper. (E) The question-setting committee must submit the questions to the chairman of the committee before Wednesday of this week.

Tongji University President Hu Requests Leave to Go to Shenyang 282

Hu Shuhua, President of Shanghai National Tongji University, requested a month's leave from the Ministry of Education yesterday to attend the annual meeting of the Chinese Engineering Society to be held in Shenyang. The university affairs will be temporarily handled by Secretary-General Tan Boyu. It is reported that the Ministry of Education has approved it.

China-France University Has Been Approved for Record Filing 283

The China-France University was initiated by people from both countries and subsidized by the governments of both countries. It was previously registered with the Ministry of Education of the Beijing government. After the establishment of the Nanjing National Government, there were some revisions to the university system. The regulations of the China-France University, which has branches at home and abroad, have all been considered and revised to ensure that they comply with the new university system, which is not as simple as that of ordinary universities, so more time is needed. During this period, the China-France University resubmitted the already registered and revised regulations for record filing with the Nanjing Education Department, which has been approved. Its treatment is completely the same as that of private universities that have been registered. In addition, the Pharmacy Specialization Department of the university has been open for just over a year, and the results have been remarkable. During the summer vacation this year, the original site at 300 Avenue Albert was greatly expanded, and many new professors were hired. A large number of various pharmaceuticals and chemical instruments were purchased from Germany. The department was jointly submitted by China-France University to the National Government Education Department for record filing and has been approved.

Sports

Sponsored by the Chinese Amateur Athletic Federation 285

International Tennis Competition

Regulations Published

The Shanghai International Tennis Competition, sponsored by the Chinese National Amateur Athletic Federation, has sent letters to sports organizations in various countries in Shanghai to invite them to participate in the competition and has stipulated the competition regulations as follows:

1. This competition will be held once a year and will adopt the World Davis Cup competition system.

2. Each country can join with one team, limited to four people.

3. The registration fee is ten yuan per team.

4. The competition will adopt a knockout system. Each match will be decided by the scores of four singles and one doubles.

5. The Spalding tennis ball is designated as the official ball for the competition.

6. The order of play will be drawn and published in various newspapers.

7. The deadline for registration is 6:00 PM on August 10th.

8. The prizes will be a large silver cup donated by the Shanghai Rotary Club, engraved with the name of the winning team each year for commemoration. The club will also donate a small silver cup each year to individual winners for encouragement.

Tennis Star Tilden's Film Arrives in Shanghai 291

World tennis star Tilden will go to Japan next month to perform tennis skills and also hopes to come to our country. It is heard that the Qianghua Company (214 Sichuan Road) has shipped Tilden's action film from the United States. The film details Tilden's serving and hitting postures and defensive strategies. Part of the film is shot in slow motion, and the tennis skills are drawn in detail step by step, which can be used as research materials for tennis lovers. Qianghua Company also sells Spalding's "Autograph" brand tennis rackets.

Shanghai Lawn Tennis Association Cancels Inter-Bank Cup 292

Chinese and Western Tennis Circles Reconcile

It is unfortunate that the Shanghai Lawn Tennis Association's refusal to allow Chinese players to join the Inter-Bank Doubles competition in this session has led to a split in opinions between Chinese and foreign tennis players. The donor of the cup clearly stated that it was for the competition of foreigners in foreign firms. It has been more than twenty years since then. Last year, the association did not object to the Chinese players joining the competition. This year, it was too late to restrict them from joining based on this provision. How could the Chinese players endure this unfairness? This is the cause of the disagreement. In short, the occurrence of this matter should be attributed to the improper handling procedures of the association's directors. The president of the association, in view of this, once invited Hu Xiansheng, chairman of the Chinese Tennis Association, and Zhou Jiaqi, secretary, for an informal conversation last week. Both parties clearly explained that they agreed that only by canceling this cup can this unfortunate event be salvaged.

Yesterday, the association held a committee meeting at the residence of the acting president, McHeel. At the same time, Hu Xiansheng, chairman of the Chinese Tennis Association, and Zhou Jiaqi, secretary, were invited to attend the meeting. After many discussions, it was publicly decided to formally cancel the Inter-Bank Cup to show that sports are open to all. The resolution of yesterday's meeting is recorded below: "The Inter-Bank Cup competition does not meet the purpose of open sports due to the limited conditions of the donor's nature. Therefore, it is resolved to cancel the cup and temporarily suspend this competition. A suitable competition should be created to replace it in the future."

Free Talk

A Laugh 293

— Sea Wanderer

Woman—Darling, I don't know why you are sometimes very brave, really like a true man, but sometimes you are so cowardly, like a woman.

Man—I'm afraid it's hereditary, because my ancestors were half male and half female.

Mother—Child, tomorrow is your tenth birthday. You can tell me what you like most, and I will definitely do it for you.

Child—I like to see the school burn down the most, so I won't be scolded by the teacher anymore.

Brother—Why don't you do serious things and just smoke cigarettes all day long?

Brother—I only have these times to smoke cigarettes, because I have to sleep all night until dawn.

Judge—Criminal, have you been to prison before?

Criminal—I haven't been to prison before, so I'm here to try something new, but you have to treat me well, otherwise, I won't come even if you send me a ticket next time.

Wife—Dear, look, the child is playing with my fox fur scarf and pulling out the fur. He cries if I don't let him play with it.

Husband—Then you can give him those kittens to play with. There are enough fur for him to pull out anyway.

Chen Duomin's Record of Resistance Against Thieves 294

— Robbery

According to a news report, a robbery occurred at the Huade Watch Store on Nanjing Road on the first of this month. The details were not clear. Because the manager of the store, Mr. Chen Duomin, is my classmate, I know more details about it, so I specially record it. The thieves, who spoke with a northern accent, were dressed in blue and white, pretending to be customers selecting gold watches. Mr. Chen Duomin cordially received them. Unexpectedly, while Mr. Chen was discussing the price with the man in white, the man in blue suddenly passed him a pistol. The transfer happened to be seen by an apprentice, so the thief bumped his jaw with his elbow. The apprentice was frightened and did not inform the store, but slipped out the back door with the intention of reporting to the police. The thief in white took the gun in his hand and openly loaded the bullets. When Mr. Chen saw this, he realized that they were thieves. Just as he was about to turn around, the thief pointed the gun at Mr. Chen's waist and threatened him not to make a sound. At the same time, the thief in blue snatched another customer's money. At this time, the shop assistants and customers were all terrified. Mr. Chen silently thought that if he let them do what they wanted, the store would suffer a major loss. He couldn't help but feel righteous indignation and disregarded everything. He quickly twisted his waist to dodge the muzzle and grabbed the thief's hand, turning the muzzle towards the thief himself. As a result, the thief in white had no way to use his skills. When the thief in blue saw that his accomplice was in trouble, he rushed to help, but the pistol had already been seized by Mr. Chen. Seeing that the situation was not good, the thief in white escaped first. Some of the shop assistants chased and shouted after him. The thief turned around and ran into the alley behind the store. Coincidentally, the apprentice of the store, who had been hit by the thief, was wandering at the entrance of the alley. When he suddenly saw the thief flying towards him, he recklessly bumped his chest with his head. The thief was taken by surprise by this sudden blow, was horrified, turned around and ran wildly to the side of Women's Bank Road, and was first captured by the apprentice. The thief in blue could not seize the gun and was no match for Mr. Chen. Seeing that his accomplice had escaped, he also ran away. Mr. Chen immediately followed with the gun and shouted for capture, and was captured by the Indian police. Looking at the capture of these two thieves this time, not only was Mr. Chen selfless, brave and decisive, but the whole store's personnel's rush to justice was also commendable. At a time when theft cases are emerging one after another, there are very few people like Mr. Chen who dare to confront thieves. Mr. Chen's bravery is enough to inject a shot in the arm for the demoralized habit. Although Mr. Chen did not have real kung fu, how could he dare to fight with his life if he had no backhand? Therefore, it is not a small contribution to the promotion of Tai Chi by the master.

A Remembrance of the Late Famous Doctor Zhou Fenbo 295

— Sun Daosheng

I remember four years ago, my father suddenly suffered from abdominal pain. It did not subside for several days. I asked many famous Chinese and Western doctors for diagnosis and treatment, but it was ineffective. I was extremely anxious. My relative, Chen Zhancheng, strongly recommended Dr. Zhou Fenbo, saying that his medical skills were excellent, and volunteered to invite him. In a short time, he came with the doctor to diagnose the illness. He described the symptoms as if he had seen them with his own eyes. The pain stopped with one dose and was completely cured with three doses. After that, whenever the old and young in my family suffered from any illness, they would seek his advice, and all were effective. Unfortunately, God did not bless people, and he suddenly returned to the mountains, which cannot but make people sigh. Fortunately, his two sons, Litang and Taihe, have been well-trained, diligently studied and practiced, and have more than enough knowledge and experience to serve the world. Their reputation is no less than that of their father. Zhu Yingpeng, a member of the Supervisory Committee of the Municipal Party Department of this city, suffered from insomnia this year. I introduced him to Dr. Litang, and he was completely cured with two doses. He exclaimed that it was a magical skill. Therefore, I believe more and more that family learning has a source and that fame and virtue must have successors.

Dr. Zhou Fenbo was originally from Wuxi and lived at No. 1 Xindeli, Nanma Road, South Wharf, Shanghai. He was always upright and had been practicing medicine for more than forty years. His prescriptions and treatments were based on the theories of Zhang Zhongjing and supplemented by the Thousand Gold Prescriptions. Therefore, his clinical diagnoses were accurate and often had miraculous effects. In recent years, he has been overworked and his qi and blood have been weakened. He often asked his two sons to diagnose instead, while he was watching by the side. This spring, I heard that he was ill and took time to visit him. I still saw that his mind was clear. He said that he had no serious illness, but that his qi and blood were weakened and he was afraid that he would not last long, but he was not afraid of death. He said that his eldest son, Litang, could continue my way, and his second son, Taihe, also had a foundation in acupuncture and throat science. If he could gain more experience, he could also serve the world. Unexpectedly, he passed away in early March. It is said that he had no remaining assets behind him, but only left ten kinds of preparations for throat problems, such as the Banzhen Pill for the Upper Moon, the Diphtheria Pill, the Infant Convulsion Powder, the Purple Gold Pill for Trauma, the Cholera Relief Pill, and special medicines for various blood conditions, such as the Chong Ren Hemorrhoid Removal Pill, the Breast Carbuncle Worry-Free Pill, the Typhoid Cinnamon Fragrance Powder, and the Miraculous Jaundice Pill. The first six types have been launched and are selling well for a while. The other four types are also being researched and will soon be available to the world. Dr. Zhou had been practicing medicine for many years and always wanted to make medicines to help patients, so he had no savings. On his deathbed, he repeatedly instructed his sons not to seek profit and to offer the legacy medicines at a fair price and provide half-price assistance to those in need to continue production and carry on his will. Dr. Zhou's uprightness, self-cultivation, and righteous methods of teaching his sons are exemplary.

Proven Remedy for Dysentery 296

— Shuping

During this intense summer heat, one careless act of eating can easily lead to dysentery, a condition of extreme danger. I recently read in a Western newspaper about a proven remedy. Although I have not tried it myself and cannot vouch for its effectiveness, I am confident it will not cause harm. Therefore, I am translating it here for your consideration.

The method involves tearing large sheets of clean, white, thick paper into small pieces and boiling them in milk for several minutes until the paper dissolves. Add a small amount of rock sugar. Take it three or four times a day. It is said that a certain doctor has been using this for thirty years with repeated remarkable effects, especially convenient and easy to implement during military campaigns. It is speculated that the dissolved white paper pulp may have the ability to moisturize and cleanse the intestines and stomach.

After Reading the "Zhonghua Tu Hua Za Zhi" (China Pictorial Magazine) 297

— Xin Er

Recently, the "Zhonghua Tu Hua Za Zhi" (China Pictorial Magazine), published by the Dongfang Publishing House, which is newly establishing a flag to promote Eastern culture, has released its inaugural issue. I originally do not understand art, but from the perspective of appreciation, after reading it several times, I found it very interesting and rich in content. Therefore, I will briefly describe its contents separately as follows:

This issue contains more than ten articles. (1) Mr. Yan Duhuo's "The Effect of Painting" is divided into three points: first, obvious; second, beautiful; and third, rich in stimulation, using simple language to explain the profound principles of the effect of painting. (2) Mr. Zhou Shoujuan's "Spring in Xuedou Mountain" is the longest and most interesting travelogue in this issue, vividly depicting the scenery, allowing the reader's mind to evoke many illusions and serene feelings of layered emerald peaks, flying waterfalls, bright breeze and clear moon, and sudden rain clouds. (3) Ms. Gao Zi's "General Evaluation of Women's Track and Field at the National Games" fully elaborates on the past advantages and disadvantages of women's track and field at the National Games and future remedies. Other articles include Mr. Wang Dafo's "A Word for the Ninth Far Eastern Games," General Chiang Kai-shek's "Ci An Ji," Zhou Shoujuan's translation of "The True Man," which can serve as an inscription for general young people, Lin Nanpeng's "A Brief Account of the Shanghai Xujiahui Observatory," which supplements public knowledge, Wu Yunmeng's "Men Are...," and Zhu Kuan's "Odds and Ends." Most of these short articles are accompanied by photographs, making them easy to understand. The textual aspect can be described as artistic.

All the pictures are full of beauty, such as Mr. Hu Boxiang's cover painting, which depicts eleven beautiful women wearing peach-red cheongsams with floral patterns, smiling and holding a small civet cat, as if嬌滴滴 (jiāodīdi, charmingly) really saying "I love little civet cat." Mr. Hu Bozhou's "Fearless Spirit" seems to portray the revolutionary masses, with the left hand supporting the party emblem and the right hand holding an iron awl, actively showing the spirit that under the blue sky and white sun, the party should be the premise and force should be the backing. In total, there are sixty or seventy photographs. In addition to current affairs photos such as "Gandhi Resisting England" and the collection of the National and Far Eastern Games and the National Boy Scout General Inspection and National Walking Group, artistic photography such as Mr. Guo Xiqi's "Consolation," Mr. Lang Jingshan's "Setting Sun," and Mr. Zhu Shouren's "Rest" are all artistic. In particular, photographs such as "Chiang Kai-shek's Hometown," "Spring in Xuedou Mountain," "Shanghai Observatory," "Construction of the People in Sichuan," and "Overseas New Inventions" are particularly valuable.

Statement: Recently, we received a letter from Mr. Tang Kaizhi of Qinghua Middle School, stating that the two drafts of Laonu, "Su Dongpo Smoking Opium," published in this publication on August 1st, have already appeared in a certain publication on the 3rd, which is obviously a case of submitting one draft to two publications. Therefore, the remuneration will be cancelled. This is hereby declared.

Random Thoughts on a Trip to the East (26) 298

— Qian Hua

(10) (9) Night Market in Ginza

The entire Tokyo Prefecture has an area of 1,389.06 square miles and a population of 4,485,144. It has two cities, one county, and eleven towns, sixty-eight villages, and one hundred and fourteen. Tokyo City is one of the two cities, with an area of 526.7 square miles and a population of 1,995,567. It is divided into fifteen districts, including the 神田 (Kanda) District, 日本橋 (Nihonbashi) District, 京橋 (Kyobashi) District, 芝 (Shiba) District, 麻布 (Azabu) District, 赤阪 (Akasaka) District, 四谷 (Yotsuya) District, 牛込 (Ushigome) District, 小石川 (Koishikawa) District, 本郷 (Hongo) District, 下谷 (Shitaya) District, 浅草 (Asakusa) District, 本所 (Honjo) District, and 深川 (Fukagawa) District. The 日本橋 (Nihonbashi) and 京橋 (Kyobashi) districts are the bustling centers, where all the banks, large companies, and corporations are gathered. There are a total of 140 banks in Tokyo City, with a total capital of 913,554,400 yen. There are 5,340 companies, with a total capital of 4,426,219,117 yen. There are 6,704 factories, with 182,205 employees. There are 646 elementary schools, with 544,312 students. In the 京橋 (Kyobashi) district, the 銀座 (Ginza) street is the most lively. The road is wide, the buildings are neat, and the multi-storied buildings are tall, similar in style to the Sassoon House in Shanghai. All the houses are uniform, without the disadvantage of unevenness. This is because the Tokyo City Hall has an overall plan for the construction of buildings. At night, the lights shine, the pedestrians are like weaving, and the vehicles are connected and driven in an orderly manner. The police maintain traffic very diligently. The speed of cars is regulated in the bustling city, with a maximum speed of 15 miles per hour. Pedestrians cross the street without any danger. News of cars injuring people is also rare. The 銀座 (Ginza) street is similar to Nanjing Road in Shanghai because of the night market, which makes it doubly lively. The Japanese value entertainment, and they always engage in various forms of recreation in their leisure time. Gambling is strictly prohibited in the country, but the 美人座 (Bijinza) dance hall, geisha houses, and mahjong clubs are very popular. As the saying goes, "If you don't gamble, you indulge in wine and women." The most noble ones take their wives and children to stroll through the night market, watching movies and dramas. The night market is open from 7 pm to 10 pm. Along both sides of the road, stalls are set up, and all kinds of goods and meals are available. The size of the stalls varies, depending on the amount of tax paid. Each stall is managed by only one person, with bamboo poles as frames and cloth awnings. Three or four colored paper lanterns are hung in front, which are strange and dazzling. From a distance, it looks like ten thousand golden snakes, which adds to the prosperity. Walking among them, examining each stall, there are clothing, antiques, calligraphy and paintings, copper and bamboo carvings, utensils, small electrical appliances, and various old goods, etc., as if entering a department store, dazzling the eyes. The Japanese production is extremely ingenious, and various Japanese mechanical products are particularly ingenious, and the price is also low, about 30-40% cheaper than those purchased in stores during the day. Therefore, the business can be maintained permanently and become a special occupation. The night market stall owners are all small-capital brokers, with only tens or hundreds of yuan of capital, which is enough to support the whole family. Half of the goods are wholesale and half are made by themselves. If they can be ingenious and invent small items, household items, or children's toys, they can occupy a superior position in the night market and earn double the profits. There are night markets in all districts, but the scale is not large. Ginza is the most prosperous, followed by Asakusa, and then Kanda, and the main products sold are different. The Ginza night market has the most clothing and silk fabrics, Asakusa has children's toys, and Kanda has more photos and books. In all the places where Japanese forces are expanding, such as Dalian and Liaoning, there are night markets, but the scale is smaller. There is also a night market outside Qianmen in Beiping, but the candlelight on the stalls is like beans, and the street lights are dim. The night market has become a black market, and the goods sold are cheap and of poor quality. Taking advantage of the darkness, unscrupulous merchants often use counterfeit goods to confuse the real ones. Customers buy them by mistake because they are greedy for cheapness, and when they see them in the light the next day, they are not worth a penny. Under the disappointment, they are annoyed. It has the name of a night market, but it is actually a black market. The Japanese night market has absolutely no fraud. The merchant's ethics are really incomparable.

Warmth in the Heart (2) (4) (9) 299

— Bao Tianxiao

Episode 13: Who Plants Good Fortune Unintentionally Obtains a Diamond Ring? Only This Predestined Relationship Can Sing of the Golden Tower with Intention

Speaking of which, Zuo Shichen smiled and said that according to your statement, I might as well not buy your tickets. Shi Guanping asked why. Zuo Shichen said that I am just an outsider who doesn't understand calligraphy, paintings, or antiques. Even if I win the lottery and get a valuable item, I would be unworthy of this rare treasure. Shi Guanping said that's not how it is. For example, if there is an exquisite painting, it is naturally best to belong to someone who can paint well and who can also write well. That way, both parties benefit. The person who paints becomes even more skilled, as the so-called "spirit is hidden in the brush and ink, and the brush and ink become spirit," and the painting also meets a soulmate, so there is no woman throwing pearls into darkness. However, even if someone cannot paint, as long as they are an appreciator, they can know the interest of the painting. After storing this painting, they can occasionally open it and play with it, as if they are in it. The colors of the trees are scattered, the mountain path is tortuous, and the thatched cottage and woodcutter's path are clear valleys and secluded streams. The scenery is not even an inch, but they can travel their eyes endlessly. At that time, although they cannot paint, the painting can be considered a soulmate for them. Otherwise, they know it is an exquisite item but can protect it carefully to wait for someone with knowledge to appreciate it, so that it will not fall into the hands of vulgar people. That can also be considered good. You know that there are now some unbearably vulgar people who don't know where they got a few stinky copper coins and want to be pretentious and buy calligraphy and paintings and ancient books to decorate their homes. In fact, they know nothing. As the so-called "full of copper stench without a single bone of elegance," if some good things fall into the hands of these people, it is really a disaster, like a beautiful woman marrying a violent, evil, and vulgar slave, which is enough to make people cry out loud. They already have such a thing, which is an undeserved blessing, but they still want to make the treasure suffer. Sometimes they inscribe a postscript that is stinky and unbearable, ruining the clean white paper. Sometimes they make a strange-shaped seal, claiming to be an appraiser of antiquity, stamping a seal in the east and stamping a seal in the west, just like putting feces on the head of a Buddha. Moreover, they stamp the seals in the vital areas, directly trying to change the fate of this antique of yours. Even if there is a good doctor, they can never cure it. Do you think this is hateful? Therefore, you blame the collectors for often keeping their precious items secret and not showing them to others, as if they are very stingy. You don't know that there are still those kinds of bad guests who fail to accomplish anything but ruin everything. Not only do they not know how to cherish them, but they also recklessly destroy them. If you are careless and lend it to them to see, they will repay you with such a prank. When you see it and shout "Oh dear," it is too late. They want to write a postscript and stamp a seal, so their name will be spread through the ancient objects, but they don't know that the treasure has suffered that disaster, that eternal disaster. Therefore, I now vow to use collotype printing to print the original ancient objects precisely, so that the original can still be treasured and the printed copy can be as good as the original and can be used for people to appreciate. Isn't that good?

However, most of the psychological autumn sales of the native yarn still have a large number of rising hopes, and the intention to do more is extremely dense. However, the business of ten and twenty native yarns is bleak.

Human Cotton Futures Continue Favorable, Five to Eight Cents Up 317

The opening price of human cotton futures yesterday was good, with robust sales continuing from the previous day. Buyer interest remained strong, and bids for each month were up by four, five, six, seven, and eight cents. The market slightly calmed down in the afternoon, with a rise of one to three cents. The total transaction volume for the day was 16,650 bales. Among the sellers, Tianchang sold the most at 1,750 bales. Other sellers included Shenxin, Maoji, Gongtai, Daji, Shenchang, Senkang, Taichang, Dechangji, Hengde, Changfeng, and Xiesheng, ranging from 200 to 1,300 bales. Among the buyers, Lichang bought the most at 1,200 bales. Other buyers included Yiyu, Taixing, Dafeng, Yuantaihe, Shenheng, Yida, Changcheng, and Yichang, ranging from 400 to 1,000 bales. Spot Yarn Prices Rise Five to Seven and a Half Cents 318

Cotton Market Strong 319

The cotton market is strong, with bullish sentiment prevailing. Private estimates of American cotton are favorable to bulls, so buyers are determined to increase their purchases. The major firm, Ruida, bought 15,000 piculs, further tightening the market. However, the weather is good for new cotton, and Japanese factories are actively selling futures cotton at flat prices.

### Han Cotton: Ruida Buys 15,000 Piculs 320

The opening price of Han cotton futures was flat. After American cotton prices declined, a major firm bought heavily, causing prices to rise by five points. In the afternoon, the yarn market was good, and retail investors expected higher prices. Market sentiment was favorable to bulls, and prices rose another two and a half cents for each month. The total transaction volume for the day was 41,300 piculs. Among the sellers, Tongyu, Tianlong, Gengfeng, Shenchang, Hengde, Taichang, Yichang, Tianchang, Dafeng, Senkang, and Xinhua Yuanda sold between 1,300 and 2,800 piculs. Private Estimates of American Cotton Reduced 323

A New York dispatch on the 5th reported that the Fuksik Bureau's estimate of the new cotton crop for this season is 66.4% of the average annual production, or 13,749,000 bales, a decrease of 701,000 bales compared to the previous estimate.

Grains: Rice Market Mixed, Firm and Weak

Zhabei 324

Yesterday, about ten boats arrived at the harbor. High-quality rice sold well in this area, while the price of average or substandard rice declined slightly. Fresh Be粳 rice was priced at around 21 yuan. The price of ordinary old rice trended downwards due to lack of demand. Large transactions were slightly reduced. Overall, rice prices fluctuated. It would be difficult to see further increase. Because the manufacturers of Dongxin粳 are inconsistent, the price increased again by half a yuan, reaching 21 yuan. The supply of Bo rice in the market is getting tighter. The price is firm and tight, with high quality rice opening at 19 yuan.

Hu Nan 325

Boats arriving are still few and sales are not good. High-quality Changxi rice remained firm due to continued price increases, but Sutong Bai rice saw weak demand and prices fell by around 0.2 yuan per unit. Warehouses of northern and southern manufacturers have sold off more than half of their inventory. Most stores are currently taking a wait-and-see approach. Current prices are still trending upward. Secondary grades of rice are moving faster. The supply of early-harvested Bo rice in Nanhui has dried up and transactions are slow, and therefore the price of rice is trending upward. Top grade rice opened at around 18 yuan.

Northern Sales of Foreign Rice Stagnant, Continuing to Fall Three to Four Cents 326

Yesterday, demand for foreign rice was weaker and more merchants are hoping for permission to ship large quantities to the north. However, in the two or three days since the ban was lifted, less than 2,000 bales have been transacted, including goods stored from before, totaling no more than 10,000 bales. Although there were reports that the Ministry of Finance would issue a second ban, Tianjin did not react. Northeast buyers did not purchase large quantities. This is because northern grain merchants have already directly purchased a large number of goods from foreign countries. These purchases are cheaper than those from Shanghai. Merchants despaired. A small portion of the merchandise was devalued in an attempt to sell, decreasing by three to four cents. The selling price opened at: No. 1 Saigon: 1,000 bags, priced at 17 yuan to 16.67 yuan; No. 2: 200 bags, priced at 14.25 yuan; Small Woven: 1,500 bags, priced at 15.8 to 15.5 yuan; Big Woven: 500 bags, priced at 12.56 yuan; Min Dang: 1,000 bags, priced at 15.4 to 15 yuan; small woven rough rice: 1,000 bags, priced at 11.6 to 11.2 yuan.

Wheat Flour Market Drastically Changes 327

The difference between high and low prices reached four cents. Shipping north remains restricted.

The wheat flour market yesterday experienced extremely large fluctuations, with the price difference being rare in recent months. When the market opened in the morning, the price of foreign wheat was good, with prices for the near term (eight or nine cents) and further out (one or two yuan) doing equally well. Market players were active, prices for the current month to October were raised by 2.57 cents. Prices for November and December were raised to 2.5675 cents, and the price for January rose to 2.5725 cents, all increasing by about four cents compared to the previous day. From the second round forward, prices declined as large factories and short sellers gradually offered resistance. Price fluctuations reached two cents. In the afternoon, it was difficult to export goods to the north, as the ban included Yantai and Qinhuangdao. Prices declined because of the ban. The price for September and October fell below the price from the previous day. This was due to speculators. The price for August and November/December did not change. The price of September/October decreased by a small amount and the price for January decreased by a smaller amount.

Wheat Futures Rise and Fall 328

Spot prices are high, one cent

Wheat futures opened higher in the morning due to higher quotes for imported wheat. The price for the current month increased to 5.0, and the price for September increased to 5.04, seven to eight points higher than the previous day. Prices in other months rose as well. As long positions pulled back, the market fell slightly. In the afternoon, prices were weak after news that flour also could not be exported. The same ban applied to ports in the north. The wheat flour market fell. As a result, the market fell. The price for August and September rose by one point compared to the previous day, October declined by one point and November to January increased by one point. Spot wheat prices were high because good quality wheat traded well and inventories were low. Traders were asking for one cent more. Fuxin acquired more than 7,000 bags of Xuzhou, Yaowan, Xinyang, Shashi, Gaoyou and Baoying wheat.

Raw Silk and Tea Prices Trend Downward 329

High inventories, stagnant sales in Europe and Japan

Excessive rainfall and fluctuating temperatures during the spring silkworm season in Jiangsu and Zhejiang provinces this year have led to a sharp increase in the production of dual cocoon silkworm cocoons. European and Japanese sales have been weak. Old stock has not been cleared. New, domestic, dual cocoon silk is continuously shipped to Shanghai. Inventories are high. The market price is low. High quality, single-cocoon double silk cocoons opened at 60 taels. A few sales were made.

Needle and Eyebrow Green Tea Sales Continued to Improve in Europe 330

Yesterday, tea merchants in Luzhuang, Zhenmei and other places were active in the tea market. The market was not idle. However, prices were still low. Dealers in Lizhuang also made some slight sales. The sales of Zhenmei were not significant. Russian buyers have been demanding lower prices for Gongxi tea. It is difficult to assess the tea market.

Textile Prices in the Midst of Huge Gains

Local Textile 331

The uptrend in textiles is very strong and sales to northern merchants have begun to pick up. Three to four hundred pieces of fine cloth and coarse cloth were transacted yesterday. Prices for fine cloth have risen by 0.075-0.05 yuan per piece. Blue Double Fish and Colored Ball fabrics are priced at 7.05 yuan and have not been priced this high in recent years. The price for Blue Chicken fabric is 6.85 yuan.

Sales of Ren Zhong balloons are doing well. Current inventories are low. Yanghe, wax figures, trumpets and other figures have only increased 0.025 yuan per piece. The prices of coarse fabrics are the most stable. Three Rabbit, Two Deer and Ren Zhong brands are selling for 4.75 yuan per piece. Blue Horse is selling for 4.6 yuan per piece. The price of fine twill has risen slightly because there have been purchases in the area.

East and West Fabrics 332

The price of fabric rose slightly. As the communist forces were gone from Changsha and demand from merchants in Tianjin increased, market sentiment trended upward. The price of fine woolen cloth, moonlight velvet rose. The prices for these textiles rose 0.0025 yuan. Lower priced Yuanzhi Gongni textiles have sold out. The current uptrend in prices may continue. The price of fabrics with deeper colored Dinghua textiles has fallen. There is an abundance of these textiles as there is a large supply. Merchant sales in Changsha have stopped. 1.95 yuan fabrics were commonly found on the market. Higher quality colored velvet yarns, glossy twill and red textiles did not change much. Bleached fabrics were stable. New flowers and Zhigongni Textiles are gaining in popularity. Western textiles have seen short supplies. The prices for fabrics have risen. The price of 1.6-chi-wide Yuan velvet yarn has increased by 0.025 yuan. The price of Taihe Theater velvet is 1.2 yuan. The difference between Yu Ling, Taixi silk and other fabrics has been large.
