European Birth Control and Promotion of Reproduction 358

— Fulan

Recently, the birth rates in various European countries have declined shockingly compared to pre-World War I levels. However, generally speaking, the number of births still exceeds the number of deaths, so government leaders in various countries are not yet overly concerned. Italy is unique in seeing an increase in its birth rate, which is a success of Mussolini's policies over the years to encourage reproduction and use other persuasive methods to attract more small citizens.

The reasons for changes in birth rates, for most European countries, are nothing more than encountering any of the following situations, or even both:

(1) The country's economic situation is too impoverished to allow the state to spend much money encouraging reproduction.

(2) The country's dense population and unemployment problems have already forced thousands of citizens to emigrate, so government offices have had to urgently and continuously implement methods to increase the population.

Central Europe

The countries of Central Europe are generally affected by both of the above situations, especially Hungary. This is because after the war, large-scale land surveys harmed 700,000 farmers, who then lived off their savings. Coupled with the decline of agriculture, this resulted in an increase of 200,000 unemployed farmers.

Social scientists believe that one hope lies in concentrating efforts on reducing infant mortality rates, the effectiveness of which is very predictable. Reliable statistics reveal that England and Russia are currently working hard on this movement. In Britain, the infant mortality rate was 148 per 1,000 in 1896, but by 1929, it had decreased to 74 per 1,000. Similarly, in Russia, it was 265 per 1,000 in 1913, but by 1928, it had also decreased to 155 per 1,000.

In Germany, the birth rate was 35.8 per 1,000 in 1901, but last year it was only 17.8 per 1,000, a decrease of more than half. According to Professor Grotjahn, a famous social scientist at the University of Berlin, he is preparing to suggest to a committee that it investigate the actual situation and begin insurance for child education and child health. However, Germany's current economic situation makes it impossible to spend millions of marks to handle this matter.

The attitudes of various European countries toward the concept of birth control vary. For example, Britain is one of the largest and strongest countries. Since 1919, the introduction of any birth control methods has been prohibited in all obstetrical schools and welfare clinics. On the other hand, abortion is legal in Russia. In that country, every effort is made to introduce all birth control methods.

A separate overview of the birth rate situation in various countries is as follows:

Germany

Unmarried men must pay 10 percent of their income in income tax. For married men without children, it is reduced to 9 percent. For married men with one child, it is reduced to 8 percent. In 1929, the number of births exceeded the number of deaths by 350,000. In 1907, the average couple had four children, but in 1929, it was only 1.97.

The current population of Germany is 60 million. Experts predict that if the current situation continues, it will definitely decrease to 46 million by 1975.

England

Currently, there are 4,131 people engaged in midwifery and welfare work in England. The infant mortality rate has been greatly reduced due to improvements in hygiene, the popularization of education, and various conveniences. Although the government does not provide bonuses, mothers can receive ten dollars from the National Health Insurance Bureau for giving birth to a child. The amounts mentioned in this article are all in US dollars for the sake of uniformity. If her husband is also insured, she can receive another ten dollars. If the father dies, the mother can receive 2.5 dollars per week for her own alimony. In addition, she receives 1.2 dollars per week for the first child and 75 cents per week for each subsequent child until they reach the age of fourteen. In 1913, the number of births in England was 881,138, but last year it was only 644,218. As in Germany, government officials claim that, given the current economic situation, it is difficult to allocate 350,000,000 dollars from the state to subsidize families, as suggested by all the Labor Party and Trade Union Congress.

France

In the first three months of this year, the number of births in France exceeded the number of deaths by 10,797. Advances in hospitals have reduced infant mortality. The government does not give bonuses to mothers, but they enjoy preferential travel expenses. If a father has 14 or 15 strong children, he often receives a very honorable commendation. In addition, the Cognac prize, with the first prize as high as 25,000 francs, is still awarded to the largest and most valuable family in the country.

Italy

Noble women linger in tea parties and banquets, while women in shacks talk about how to care for infants. Mussolini cannot escape blame for this. He was alarmed by the drop in the birth rate, believing that it was a sign of national decline. Therefore, three years ago, he hurriedly encouraged reproduction in order to increase the number of young Italian citizens. He used various incentives. Based on the birth rate in the first six months of this year, the national population will reach 43 million by 1931. In other words, it will increase by 650,000 in one year, an increase of 30 percent compared to the pre-war average birth rate of 500,000 per year. When Mussolini's first decree was issued in 1927, the funds he used to improve children's welfare and midwifery came entirely from taxes on unmarried men. In addition, he exhausted all kinds of methods to prevent birth control. All propaganda of this kind is not allowed. Pharmacies may not prepare birth control prescriptions without a doctor's order. He often withheld funds for local public works improvements, instructing officials to start work as soon as the population increased.

Russia

Soviet Russia has the highest mortality rate in Europe. In 1928, there were 42 births per 1,000 people and 18.1 deaths per 1,000 people. As a result, the population still naturally increased by 3.5 million. In state schools, trade union members are educated about birth control free of charge. Once a woman proves that she is pregnant, a government-established committee can order a legal abortion. However, this situation leads to many illegal actions. In addition to the government's efforts to promote birth control, it seems to be desperately encouraging the success of large families. Working-class mothers have two months of full leave before and after childbirth without deducting wages. Many large factories have set up nurses and nannies to take care of children while their mothers are working. According to the current population growth situation, Russia will have 300 million people by 1960.

Hungary

Although Hungary now has a larger population than it can support, many people still feel the decline in the birth rate and are eager to encourage reproduction. The government prepares excellent hospitals and sanatoriums for mothers, providing them with free milk and medical assistance to ensure that the birth of children does not burden families with any expenses.

Poland

The continuous population increase in this country is indeed a heavy burden. In the five years before World War I, Poland was one of the countries with the highest birth rate in Europe, second only to Russia and the countries of Central Europe. Currently, the birth rate is 34 per 1,000, and the number of marriages is decreasing year by year.

Belgium

The birth rate in Belgium is falling rapidly, and the decline has not stopped. In 1880, it was 31.1 per 10,000, but by 1927 it had fallen by 41 percent. Currently, an organization has been established where fathers can borrow money without interest. Many educational institutions have government subsidies so that children have the opportunity to receive education. Government employees with families have their travel expenses reduced or their wages slightly increased. All these efforts are nothing more than encouraging the increase of small citizens.

Spain

This country rarely takes action to encourage reproduction. The former dictator, Primo de Rivera, once approved a small amount of assistance to be given to helpless families with eight or more children, but this was only limited to relieving poverty. Because it is a Catholic country, any form of birth control and propaganda is strictly prohibited. Its birth rate was 35.7 per 1,000 in 1887, but by 1928 it was only 29.6 per 1,000.

Portugal

The infant mortality rate is very high, and the punishment for implementing birth control is quite severe. Its number of births is equal to the number of deaths and immigrants. In 1918, it was 34.6 per 1,000, and in 1928 it was 31.

Czechoslovakia

The population is overpopulated, and birth control is unknown. In 1926, there were 344,000 births and 219,149 deaths. The government provides free medical assistance for those who implement fertility treatment, while it is considering drafting a law to punish those who implement birth control. The contradictions of measures are like this.

Austria

The number of births exceeds the number of deaths. Although it does not encourage birth control, the government does not prohibit it either. Birth control devices are sold everywhere. In Vienna alone, there are 200 nursing homes that send representatives to the homes of reproducing mothers at any time to observe whether they are receiving appropriate medical care. In addition, there is a social insurance payment given to mothers as soon as her baby is born, and a basket of baby clothes is given as a gift. If the mother has to work during the day, the kindergarten also has very detailed regulations for the care of children. When children reach the age of six, they can play and escape the summer heat in healthy farms that are half-subsidized by the government.

Scandinavian Countries

The countries on this peninsula pay little attention to birth rates. In Sweden, it fell from 23.1 per 1,000 in 1913 to 16 in 1928. Denmark fell from 25.6 to 19.6. Finland fell from 27.1 to 23.2. Norway fell from 24.9 to 17.7.

Shanghai Plans to Build International Radio 359

Adopts Domestically Made Transformers

The international radio station is a very important communication facility among international entities. The power station is located in Zhenru, and the project is very large. The electrical capacity used is 400 kVA. Two huge transformers are installed, which are constructed by the local Yizhong Machinery Company. They are currently being installed. The entire project is expected to be completed around September. This is truly good news about domestically made electrical machinery.

(1) The text should be limited to news about domestic and foreign science, industry, commerce, rural areas, health, aviation, exploration, customs, or urban life.

(2) The pictures should be limited to various lyrical paintings about social life.

The Vanguard Weekly, Issue 7 361

The Vanguard Weekly, Issue 7, published by the Vanguard Society, was published yesterday. The main contents include (1) War, (2) White Horse Mountain, (3) After Unemployment, (4) Our Own People (Poetry), and (5) Two Orphans, all of which are very exciting, especially the War article, which is the most eye-catching. Sales locations in this city include bookstores such as Kaiming, Zhenmei, Shan, Jinwu, Modern Guanghua, and Daguang, New Life, etc. and major bookstores in other cities.

The founding issue of Era Youth, published by the Era Youth Society, was published yesterday. The main contents include "Anatomy of Modern Chinese Youth Pathology," "A Bird's-Eye View of the Anti-Imperialist Movement of Weak and Small Nations in the World," "The Way Out for the Chinese Nation to Seek Freedom and Equality," "Exclusively in Front of the Era Youth," "Our Understanding of Literature and Art in the Future," "Marching Forward for the Nation," and "Era Youth." Sales locations are Ximen Daguang Bookstore, all school gatehouses, and all newspaper vendors.

Wilderness Weekly Renovation Issue 363

— Jin Ding

Published by the Wilderness Society

I have a fondness for small publications, especially those with a literary focus. Wilderness Weekly is of course one of my favorite reads because its content is definitely not "tabloidized" like most of the current publications circulating in society, at least in terms of writing. From my objective perspective, the past Wilderness lacked a consistent theme because the thoughts of the various authors were not unified. Each author stood on their own ground and expressed themselves. Although we didn't find it monotonous, it gave us a confusing and strange impression in terms of thought and failed to show the entire center of Wilderness. This was really his only defect in the past. The first volume of Wilderness can be said to be his germination period. The content generally could not get rid of immaturity and superficiality, but this is a necessary phenomenon when general magazines are first created. Wilderness in the early stage was of course unavoidable. The second volume of Wilderness can be said to be his growth period. The content gradually seemed to fill up like the body of a young adult. This is obviously the result of the efforts of the journal's editors and society members to have such achievements, which cannot be regarded as success. However, it can be said to be unique among small publications. The recently published Wilderness Renovation Issue (i.e., Volume 3, Issue 1) has actually progressed from the growth period to the prosperity period. After reading it, I immediately felt that the content has been completely renewed. Taking nationalist literature and art as the central idea of the journal, there is an invisible unity in the writing, which leaves a deep image in our minds, which is a world apart from the previous two volumes. Now I'll take some free time to introduce this issue of Wilderness.

"The Expression and Imagination of National Literature and Art" This thesis was written by Tang Zengyang. As far as I know, the author has done a lot for the past Wilderness, and at the same time, he has a considerable success in poetics. The author first determined the central idea of ​​literature and art at the opening of the article, and made a brief examination of the long-term growth of national consciousness literature and art in ancient China. Readers can understand the history of folk thoughts in the national process. Secondly, the "expression" method and "imagination" elements of national literature and art are described systematically, and it is discussed that "imagination" is by no means "fantasy" Fancy. There is also a concrete explanation of this.

"The Last Strike" This creation was written by Wang Tiehua. People who have read Wilderness can mostly know that he is the editor of the journal. His creative novels are actually superior to other types. This is a general observation of Wilderness readers, at least I feel it myself. "The Last Strike" is divided into five paragraphs, with the tumultuous Sino-Russian incident as the background of the article. It can also be said that historical facts are used as the facts. The author used all his energy to express the personality and intense patriotism of the important protagonist Zhao Lianchang in this article, prompting his only fourteen-year-old son to also do his best for the country. When he knew that his illness was difficult to cure, he still said to his son passionately: "You, Ying, you must remember my words. You are not too young at the age of fourteen. If I die, I cannot arrange your future. In short, you must not forget my death and the wounds of my country. You must use your strength to rush. Even if you become a road worker in the future, you must transport bullets to the front to kill the bandits..." From this, it can be seen that his love for the country is more intense than his love for his son. In terms of technique, the author has achieved great success. In the first paragraph, when Zhao Lianchang was angry with his son, he described a broken table in the room with two bottles, which made a mutual striking sound due to the vibration of the bed. The last strike was to write about the situation of Russian soldiers harassing the town. When the Russian soldiers rushed up the small building triumphantly, only small bottles were shaking on the broken table. Finally, the author pointed out that "a pile of glass bottle fragments were found downstairs" implying that this was Zhao Lianchang struggling to use the strength of his death to pick up the small bottles and make the "last strike" at the Russian soldiers who were committing atrocities in order to express his patriotic and brave heart. This is really the technique of creation, and the author's expression is also superior to other creations that write "ordinary stories". It is a great joy to be able to read such a powerful novel with nationalism as the center on a small Wilderness. In terms of structure, the article seems to be hasty. This shows that the author may have initially prepared to write a long or medium-length creation. Now that it has been reduced to a short story, it is not impossible. On the contrary, the whole article feels compact. But I hope that the author can develop the article into a powerful long story based on true facts so that the people of the country can know how the Soviet Russia, which claims to support the weak, is acting violently and illegally in China, awakening the national consciousness of the people of the country.

Such as the literary news and other things, it is possible to deeply imprint the whole literary news and inside information of China and the actions and tendencies of various writers in this very short news, and make a brief report with an objective perspective, and most of the things published are indeed reliable. This is really worthy of praise.

In short, in this Wilderness Renovation Issue, authors have all obtained the central idea in terms of thought and objectivity, and the writing has gradually created unity, so that readers who love the journal also get correct instructions invisibly and become a must-read literary publication for young people. According to reporters, the future direction of the company is worthy of attention by those who care about Wilderness. The two sections are now excerpted below as the end of the introduction of this article.

In terms of content, we will strive to enrich it in the future. Both the submissions from society members and external submissions will be strictly selected. If there is no good manuscript worth reading, we would rather leave a lot of blank space in this journal, and at the same time, we will never cater to the low-level tastes of readers. In terms of form, we have also tried our best to change the so-called "tabloidization" from this issue, because our Wilderness plans to make a considerable contribution to young people who are studying literature and art and not to be a kind of pastime for "idle" friends after tea and wine. Therefore, we are willing to keep the sales of Wilderness at its level or even reduce it.

In terms of writing, it is extremely important to make it have a consistent unity and determine the central idea, which is of course the central idea of ​​nationalism. We will not be polite to reject deformed and pathological literature and art. If there is someone who can stand on the same front and work together to promote national literature and art, we hope that he can join hands with Wilderness, otherwise, we hope that he will go his own way. The future Wilderness will not allow the so-called speculative, fence-sitting, divergent, etc. factors without a central consciousness.

Wilderness Weekly, published by the Wilderness Society, was published last Saturday, Volume 3, Issue 2. The content is even richer than the previous Renovation Issue. The sales locations are newspaper vendors and school gatehouses. Attach two cents for postage and immediate delivery.

Group News 365

After the Purple Opera Troupe decided to tour Xiamen in the 19th year, after more than a month of preparation, they left Shanghai on July 17 and arrived in Xiamen. After a short rest, they met with local people on stage. The plays performed were Ibsen's A Doll's House, Chekhov's The Boor, Maeda Kawakoichiro's The Death of Rasputin, Marinetti's Let's Go!, and Shao Wei's The Unknown Son. The five plays were performed in three days and four scenes and were well received by local people. Now, except for Xiang Peiliang and Shao Wei, who still need to stay in Xiamen for a few days due to business, the other members of the troupe, Yang Lukun, Hu Manqian, Liu Zhongda, Wang Bingxin, Hu Anhui, Zhou Zushang, Zhong Jingkang, Yao Yuxuan, Luo Songbai, Guo Li, Zhou Tianran, Li Pingfen, Wang Zenong, and other thirteen people all returned to Shanghai on the Taiyuan ship on August 1. It is said that the people arrived in port the day before yesterday.

Commercial News 366

The Shanghai Commercial Office of Shaoxing Huaxing Cement Mine Preparation Office was established yesterday. The initiators are Xie Yiou, Lu Wen'an, Liu Daofang, Wang Shipeng, and more than a dozen others. The mine is located in Lougong, 20 miles away from Pianmen in Shaoxing. The mineral deposits reach more than 3,000 acres. The chemical test results show that it is pure white cement. The mining machinery and construction of a light railway for transporting goods require 3 million shares. The overseas Chinese investment is being actively discussed, and leading figures of the National Government are being sought to join the sponsorship. The Preparation Office issued a declaration yesterday, recording that the most important thing for starting a business is to invest in mining, and the key to utilizing and promoting life lies in the opening of production enterprises. The wealth of agriculture and mines in our country is surpassed by various countries. The great powers are watching closely and pinning their hopes on the abundance of mineral deposits in our country. Tracing back to the decline of production, the decline of industry and commerce, the withering of the economy, and the spread of vagrants in our country, which is a major disaster for society. The root cause is that the people of the country do not engage in the promotion of production enterprises, and the national economy and people's livelihood are both weak and in trouble. It is worrying. The social state of our country has always attached importance to industrial and commercial enterprises, and there are very few facilities for agricultural and mining plans. Even if one or two initiators feel that it is difficult to gather strong investments, they give up eating because of choking, which is always regrettable. Now, overseas Chinese are concerned about the people's livelihood construction of the motherland, organizing industrial groups and returning to the country to inspect the state of industry, investing in mining and promoting profitable enterprises. Recently, the Ministry of Industry and Commerce of the National Government convened a national industrial and commercial conference to encourage industrial and commercial policies, promote the development of production enterprises, increase foreign trade, and increase the national economy. Colleagues and others have personally met at this time, and they have not hesitated to initiate the Shaoxing Huaxing Cement Factory Co., Ltd., which is run by Zhejiang merchants, and set up a general preparation office in Shanghai to start preparations. Its mine is located in Lougong, 20 miles away from Pianmen in Shaoxing County, Zhejiang Province, named Lion Mountain. The mountain's cliffs are dangerous and connected like a snake. The total area of the mountain reaches more than 3,000 acres. The base of the mountain belongs to the Huizao Head Village in the territory. The villagers gather to take stone scraps and earth to burn and manufacture lime, which is white and strong, and is supplied to the entire Zhejiang for the needs of the architectural engineering. It is regarded as the top product. The general public in the village relies on this for their livelihood. They have been working hard for many years, generation after generation, like the foolish old man moving mountains. Since the opening of mining in the sixteenth year of Qianlong, it has been going on for more than 200 years, only cutting off one corner of the mountain end. The substance of 15% of its entire area has a long history. Colleagues and others have repeatedly invited well-known mining experts from various countries to test the results separately. The mineral quality is pure white cement, and the test results show that the output rate can be supplied to the construction of the world on a large scale. It can be called a giant mine. It is planned to raise 3 million shares to start the business. The purpose of the colleagues is to open up production, develop industrial and commercial enterprises, promote the realization of the policy of economic assistance and the people's livelihood and doctrine, and contribute to the society. It is hoped that the leading figures of our party and country, social leaders, industrial and commercial experts, and industrial leaders will participate in and assist in the success of the country and benefit the people.

The China Sanitary Pepper Machine Powder Company at the intersection of Baike Road and Renhe Lane previously submitted an application to the Shanghai Municipal Social Bureau for registration in accordance with the company regulations. Because the articles of association were not in compliance, they were returned for revision. They immediately followed the amendments and re-applied for registration. Now, the Social Bureau has approved it and issued Approval Order No. 9366. After receiving the approval, the company has already started trading in accordance with the law. All Chinese and Western restaurants in this city have the sanitary pepper powder produced by the company for the use of diners.

Theater News 367

The Beijing Grand Theater announces that the theater is currently undergoing a complete renovation, with the interior corridors and the theater itself being newly decorated in a magnificent and resplendent manner. In addition, equipment such as projectors and screens will also be newly installed, which is expected to be completed in about half a month.

The Baixing Grand Theater announces that, starting from the 2nd of this month, the theater has hired the famous Shanghai Sisters' Dance Troupe to perform the latest and most innovative variety of songs and dances at every performance, both day and night. Therefore, the outdoor screening at 9:15 PM has been moved downstairs. This troupe is organized by the film star Ms. Liang Saizhen and is renowned in the artistic world. The Charleston dance of the three sisters, Liang Saizhu, Liang Saishan, and Liang Saihu, is very popular and well-known in Shanghai. The other actors are also the best of their time. The recent performance of "Butterfly Girl" by Saizhu and Saishan has been very successful, with almost no empty seats. It is indeed the most prosperous season the theater has ever had.

The Xifan Film Company announces that all the craftsmen of the company's engineering department have gone to Ningbo South Township to build more than ten houses in the new film "Golden Rooster Ridge" to prepare for the real scene of the "Burning of the Diao Family Village" in the play. The scenery is exceptionally grand and realistic. The company's photography team will also set off soon to set fire to these houses.

The Mingxing Film Company announces that the company's director, Cheng Bugao, has completed the filming of "Romantic Woman" with all his effort and will soon release it at the Central Theater. It is learned that Mr. Cheng is also working on a new script written by Mr. Zhang Shichuan, who named it "A Prostitute's Precious Mother." Director Cheng has completed the distribution of male and female leads and important actors. The female lead is Xuan Jinglin, the male lead is Wang Jiting, and others such as Gong Jianong, Huang Junfu, and Tan Zhiyuan are also important roles in the film. Filming began yesterday.

The Hongkou Grape Dance Troupe announces that, in order to revive the dance movement, the troupe will hold a large-scale public performance at the New Oriental Theater on North Sichuan Road, near the Yokohama Bridge, on August 16th. The confirmed programs include "Grape Fairy," "Three Butterflies," and "Little Painter" by Mr. Li Jinhui, as well as "Sentiments," "Annoyance," and "King of Fragrance" created by Mr. Lai Linshu of the troupe, and the romantic opera "Moonlight Serenade" and "Purple Grapes" by Miss Luo Weier. In order to expand publicity, the troupe will issue a beautifully illustrated publication dedicated to pictures and photos of the revival of the dance movement. In addition to inviting major dance artists in Shanghai to contribute articles, the troupe also plans to solicit comments from the public. Selected articles will be published and rewarded handsomely. Please send manuscripts to the Editorial Department of the "Revival of Dance Movement" illustrated publication at 170 Yuqing Lane, North Sichuan Road.

The Changming Film Company announces that the first episode of "Burning Pingyang City," directed by Yang Xiaozhong, was released in the Central Theater in the spring. The photography, plot, and scenery were able to attract the audience's attention, so the public opinion was excellent, and the box office performance was no less than "Red Lotus Temple." Recently, Yang Xiaozhong and Chen Zhiqing have continued their painstaking work with the second episode. The filming methods in this episode are particularly rare and bizarre, which are more admirable than the first episode. As for the plot of the second episode, because the first episode was the introduction of the characters, there was no tortuous plot to narrate. The second episode is the opening of the story, and the highlights are seen at the beginning. The filming of this film has been completed for a long time and will be released in the Central Theater soon. Please wait and see.

Medical News 368

The Yuan Dong Jian Hua Li Foreign Firm at the end of North Zhejiang Road announces that the French Sheng Sheng Ling, managed by this firm, is a special medicine for the relief of severe kidney failure in men. Recently, affected by the gold rush, the cost price has exceeded the original price by one time. After the existing stock is sold out, it will be sold at the newly set price. It is currently still sold at two yuan per bottle, which is expected to last for about three or four weeks.

The Nanyang Pharmacy announces that since this pharmacy moved to the entrance of Zhonghong Temple Lane on Nanjing Road, the business has been booming. Recently, it has also invited Ms. Li Mucheng, the daughter of the famous Lingnan doctor Yang Yizhi, to set up a clinic on the second floor. Therefore, people from Chaozhou and Meizhou have been flocking to the clinic. Both doctors have a solid foundation of knowledge and rich experience, and the medicines and instruments used are particularly precious. The daily consultation hours are from 10:00 to 12:00 in the morning. Dr. Yang is from Shantou and graduated from the Beiyang Army Medical School. He has served as the epidemic prevention medical officer of the Chaozhou Customs, the director of the military hospital of the Second Town of Beiyang and the Second Division of Guangdong, the naval medical officer of the Hai琛 warship, the director of the Moderen Charity Hospital, and the founder of the Shantou Nanli Chaozhou Obstetrics School and Women's Hospital. He is proficient in internal and external medicine and has particularly exquisite treatment methods for venereal diseases, tuberculosis, and hemorrhoids. Dr. Li has served as a doctor and teacher at the Shantou Gospel Women's Hospital for more than ten years, and the director of obstetrics at the Chaozhou Obstetrics School and the medical director of the Women's Hospital. She is proficient in women's and children's diseases.

Masseuse Ms. Ma Yushu announces that this medical practitioner has been studying pediatric massage for more than 20 years and has saved many children in the French Concession of Shanghai. The secret methods that she has learned and mastered have been compiled into a book called "Massage Shortcuts," which has been published and is available to the public. The content is rich, the illustrations are detailed, and the wording is simple. Therefore, buyers have been rushing to buy it every day. This book is sold at bookstores such as the Huatong Chinese Medicine Bookstore in this city.
